```java
    public void voidOrder(Long transferId) {
        TransferEntity bill = transferRepository.getById(transferId);
        TransferValidation.validVoidOrder(bill);
        List<TransferItemEntity> items = transferRepository.listItemsByBillId(transferId);

        InventoryUnifiedOutboundContext outContext = InventoryUnifiedConvert.toOutboundContext(bill, items,
            bill.getTargetWarehouseId(), bill.getTargetWarehouseName(), BusinessTypeEnum.TRANSFER_VOID_REVERSE_OUT.getCode());
        inventoryUnifiedService.decreaseStockByOutboundContext(outContext);

        InventoryUnifiedInboundContext inContext = InventoryUnifiedConvert.toInboundContext(bill, items,
            bill.getSourceWarehouseId(), bill.getSourceWarehouseName(), BusinessTypeEnum.TRANSFER_VOID_REVERSE_IN.getCode());
        inventoryUnifiedService.increaseStockByInboundContext(inContext);

        bill.setStatus(OrderStatusEnum.CANCELLED.getCode());
        transferRepository.updateById(bill);
    }
}
```

**5.2.8.5 调用关系小结**

| 业务 | 正向 | 逆向（作废） |
|------|------|-------------|
| 采购入库单 | `approveInbound` → 构建 `InventoryUnifiedInboundContext`(PURCHASE_IN) → `increaseStockByInboundContext` | `voidOrder` → 构建 `InventoryUnifiedOutboundContext`(PURCHASE_IN_VOID) → `decreaseStockByOutboundContext` |
| 调拨单 | `approveOutbound` → `InventoryUnifiedOutboundContext`(TRANSFER_OUT) → `decreaseStockByOutboundContext`<br/>`approveInbound` → `InventoryUnifiedInboundContext`(TRANSFER_IN) → `increaseStockByInboundContext` | `voidOrder` → `InventoryUnifiedOutboundContext`(TRANSFER_VOID_REVERSE_OUT) → `decreaseStockByOutboundContext`<br/>→ `InventoryUnifiedInboundContext`(TRANSFER_VOID_REVERSE_IN) → `increaseStockByInboundContext` |

- `InventoryUnifiedServiceImpl` 实现 `InventoryUnifiedService` 接口，只负责按上下文更新 `inventory` 和写流水，不关心业务类型。
- 采购、调拨等业务服务负责：构建上下文 → 调用统一服务 → 更新单据状态。

**重构原则应用**：
- **Introduce Parameter Object**：`writeInventoryItem` 原 12 个参数聚合为 `InventoryItemWriteCommand`，便于扩展（新增字段只需改 DTO）、降低耦合、提升可读性
- **Single Responsibility**：`InventoryItemWriteCommand` 仅承载流水写入所需数据，职责单一
- **Open/Closed**：后续若需增加流水字段（如批次号、成本等），只需扩展 Command，无需改方法签名
- **Converter Layer**：`InventoryItemConvert` 负责 Command 构建（`toWriteCommand`）与 Command→Entity 转换（`toEntity`），Service 只调用转换与持久化，符合分层规范

---

## 5. 核心逻辑实现

### 5.1 库存管理逻辑

#### 5.1.1 核心设计理念

**关键原则**：
1. **底层统一**：所有库存更新都通过统一入库单/出库单处理
2. **展示分离**：对外展示时体现原始业务单据类型（采购入库单、销售出库单、调拨单等）
3. **追溯完整**：库存流水日志记录完整的业务上下文，包括原始业务类型和单据号
4. **设计模式解耦**：通过适配器、门面、策略等设计模式实现业务层与库存层的解耦（详见 [设计模式应用文档](./库存管理系统设计模式应用.md)）
5. **DDD聚合根设计**：通过领域驱动设计的聚合根概念，聚合库存管理和批次管理的核心业务行为（详见 [DDD聚合根设计文档](./库存管理系统DDD聚合根设计.md)）

**设计模式应用**：
- **适配器模式**：统一入库单/出库单作为适配器，将各种业务单据适配为统一的库存更新接口
- **门面模式**：`InventoryUnifiedService`作为门面，为业务层提供简化的库存操作接口
- **策略模式**：FIFO扣减策略，可扩展为LIFO、平均成本等策略
- **模板方法模式**：统一的库存更新流程模板
- **观察者模式**：库存变更事件发布，实现解耦的后续处理

**DDD聚合根设计**：
- **库存管理聚合**：`Inventory`作为聚合根，封装库存增减、分配等业务行为
- **批次管理聚合**：`Batch`作为聚合根，封装批次创建、FIFO扣减、资源纳入等业务行为
- **聚合间协作**：通过应用服务（统一入库单/出库单）协调多个聚合的操作

**核心流程**：
```
业务单据（采购入库单/销售出库单/调拨单等）
    ↓
在代码层转换为统一入库/出库上下文（InventoryUnifiedInboundContext / InventoryUnifiedOutboundContext）
   （上下文携带：业务类型、单据类型、单据号、仓库、明细等；不落统一单据表）
    ↓
调用统一库存更新服务（传入上下文），更新 inventory 表
    ↓
写入库存流水（bill_inventory_item），business_type、bill_type、bill_id、bill_code 取自上下文
    ↓
对外展示库存流水时，显示原始业务类型（采购入库、销售出库、调拨入库、调拨出库等）
```

**关键点**：
- ✅ 数据库层不建统一单据表；代码层用「上下文」驱动库存更新与流水记录
- ✅ 上下文（或等价 DTO）必须包含 `business_type`、`bill_type`、`bill_id`、`bill_code` 等追溯信息
- ✅ 记录库存流水时，从上下文中取值写入 `bill_inventory_item`，保证可追溯
- ✅ 新增业务单据时，通过「上下文构建器 + 注册表」扩展，不修改统一库存服务（详见 5.2.5）

### 5.2 业务单据到统一入库/出库上下文的转换逻辑

**实现约定（与数据库设计一致）**：数据库层**不建**统一单据表及统一单据明细表。下述“转换”产出应为**内存中的统一入库/出库上下文**（`InventoryUnifiedInboundContext` / `InventoryUnifiedOutboundContext`），业务层构建上下文后调用 `InventoryUnifiedService.increaseStockByInboundContext(context)` / `decreaseStockByOutboundContext(context)`，由统一库存服务直接更新 `inventory` 并写入 `bill_inventory_item` 流水。下文的 Convert/Entity 示例仅说明**各业务单据应组装哪些字段**（如 business_type、bill_type、bill_id、bill_code、仓库、明细），实际实现时用 Context DTO 替代 Entity，**不要**再执行 `insertUnifiedInboundOrder` / `insertUnifiedOutboundOrder` 等落库操作。

#### 5.1.2.1 枚举类定义

```java
/**
 * 单据状态枚举
 */
@Getter
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public enum OrderStatusEnum {
    
    DRAFT("DRAFT", "草稿"),
    PENDING("PENDING", "待审核"),
    APPROVED("APPROVED", "已审核"),
    INBOUNDED("INBOUNDED", "已入库"),
    PENDING_OUTBOUND("PENDING_OUTBOUND", "待出库"),
    IN_TRANSIT("IN_TRANSIT", "运输中"),
    COMPLETED("COMPLETED", "已完成"),
    SHIPPED("SHIPPED", "已发货"),
    CANCELLED("CANCELLED", "已取消");
    
    private final String code;
    private final String desc;
    
    public static OrderStatusEnum findByCodeOrThrow(String code) {
        return java.util.Arrays.stream(values())
            .filter(e -> e.getCode().equals(code))
            .findFirst()
            .orElseThrow(() -> new BusinessException("不识别的单据状态: " + code));
    }
}

/**
 * 业务类型枚举
 */
@Getter
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public enum BusinessTypeEnum {
    
    PURCHASE_IN("PURCHASE_IN", "采购入库"),
    TRANSFER_IN("TRANSFER_IN", "调拨入库"),
    TRANSFER_OUT("TRANSFER_OUT", "调拨出库"),
    SALES_OUT("SALES_OUT", "销售出库"),
    BATCH_ADJUSTMENT("BATCH_ADJUSTMENT", "批次调整"),
    INVENTORY_ADJUSTMENT("INVENTORY_ADJUSTMENT", "库存调整"),
    ALLOCATE("ALLOCATE", "分配"),
    DEALLOCATE("DEALLOCATE", "取消分配");
    
    private final String code;
    private final String desc;
    
    public static BusinessTypeEnum findByCodeOrThrow(String code) {
        return java.util.Arrays.stream(values())
            .filter(e -> e.getCode().equals(code))
            .findFirst()
            .orElseThrow(() -> new BusinessException("不识别的业务类型: " + code));
    }
}

/**
 * 单据类型枚举
 */
@Getter
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public enum DocumentTypeEnum {
    
    IN("IN", "采购入库单"),
    TR("TR", "调拨单"),
    ORD("ORD", "销售出库单"),
    BATCH("BATCH", "批次"),
    UIO("UIO", "统一入库单"),
    UOO("UOO", "统一出库单");
    
    private final String code;
    private final String desc;
    
    public static DocumentTypeEnum findByCodeOrThrow(String code) {
        return java.util.Arrays.stream(values())
            .filter(e -> e.getCode().equals(code))
            .findFirst()
            .orElseThrow(() -> new BusinessException("不识别的单据类型: " + code));
    }
}

/**
 * 产品状态枚举
 */
@Getter
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public enum ProductStatusEnum {
    
    NORMAL("正品", "正品"),
    DEFECTIVE("次品", "次品");
    
    private final String code;
    private final String desc;
    
    public static ProductStatusEnum findByCodeOrThrow(String code) {
        return java.util.Arrays.stream(values())
            .filter(e -> e.getCode().equals(code))
            .findFirst()
            .orElseThrow(() -> new BusinessException("不识别的产品状态: " + code));
    }
}
```

#### 5.1.2.2 统一单转换类（Convert）

```java
/**
 * 统一入库单转换类
 * 
 * 职责：
 * 1. 将业务单据转换为统一入库单
 * 2. 统一转换逻辑，避免重复代码
 */
public final class UnifiedInboundOrderConvert {
    
    /**
     * 从采购入库单转换为统一入库单
     */
    public static UnifiedInboundOrderEntity fromPurchaseInOrder(
            PurchaseInOrderEntity purchaseOrder,
            DocumentNumberService documentNumberService) {
        
        UnifiedInboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = new UnifiedInboundOrderEntity();
        unifiedOrder.setOrderNumber(documentNumberService.generateUnifiedInboundOrderNumber());
        unifiedOrder.setSourceDocumentType(BusinessTypeEnum.PURCHASE_IN.getCode());
        unifiedOrder.setSourceDocumentId(purchaseOrder.getOrderNumber());
        unifiedOrder.setWarehouseId(purchaseOrder.getTargetWarehouseId());
        unifiedOrder.setBusinessDate(purchaseOrder.getBusinessDate());
        unifiedOrder.setStatus(OrderStatusEnum.COMPLETED.getCode());
        
        return unifiedOrder;
    }
    
    /**
     * 从调拨单转换为统一入库单（目标仓库）
     */
    public static UnifiedInboundOrderEntity fromTransferOrderInbound(
            TransferOrderEntity transferOrder,
            DocumentNumberService documentNumberService) {
        
        UnifiedInboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = new UnifiedInboundOrderEntity();
        unifiedOrder.setOrderNumber(documentNumberService.generateUnifiedInboundOrderNumber());
        unifiedOrder.setSourceDocumentType(BusinessTypeEnum.TRANSFER_IN.getCode());
        unifiedOrder.setSourceDocumentId(transferOrder.getOrderNumber());
        unifiedOrder.setWarehouseId(transferOrder.getDestinationWarehouseId());
        unifiedOrder.setBusinessDate(transferOrder.getBusinessDate());
        unifiedOrder.setStatus(OrderStatusEnum.COMPLETED.getCode());
        
        return unifiedOrder;
    }
    
    /**
     * 从采购入库单明细转换为统一入库单明细
     */
    public static UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity fromPurchaseInOrderItem(
            PurchaseInOrderItemEntity item,
            Long unifiedOrderId,
            String sourceOrderNumber) {
        
        UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity unifiedItem = new UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity();
        unifiedItem.setUnifiedInboundOrderId(unifiedOrderId);
        unifiedItem.setProductId(item.getProductId());
        unifiedItem.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
        unifiedItem.setQuantity(item.getQuantity());
        unifiedItem.setUnit(item.getUnit());
        unifiedItem.setBusinessType(BusinessTypeEnum.PURCHASE_IN.getCode());
        unifiedItem.setRelatedDocumentType(DocumentTypeEnum.IN.getCode());
        unifiedItem.setRelatedDocumentId(sourceOrderNumber);
        
        return unifiedItem;
    }
    
    /**
     * 从调拨单明细转换为统一入库单明细（目标仓库）
     */
    public static UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity fromTransferOrderItemInbound(
            TransferOrderItemEntity item,
            Long unifiedOrderId,
            String sourceOrderNumber) {
        
        UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity unifiedItem = new UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity();
        unifiedItem.setUnifiedInboundOrderId(unifiedOrderId);
        unifiedItem.setProductId(item.getProductId());
        unifiedItem.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
        unifiedItem.setQuantity(item.getTransferQuantity());
        unifiedItem.setUnit(item.getUnit());
        unifiedItem.setBusinessType(BusinessTypeEnum.TRANSFER_IN.getCode());
        unifiedItem.setRelatedDocumentType(DocumentTypeEnum.TR.getCode());
        unifiedItem.setRelatedDocumentId(sourceOrderNumber);
        
        return unifiedItem;
    }
    
    /**
     * 批量转换采购入库单明细
     */
    public static List<UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity> fromPurchaseInOrderItems(
            List<PurchaseInOrderItemEntity> items,
            Long unifiedOrderId,
            String sourceOrderNumber) {
        
        return items.stream()
            .map(item -> fromPurchaseInOrderItem(item, unifiedOrderId, sourceOrderNumber))
            .collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.toList());
    }
    
    /**
     * 批量转换调拨单明细（入库）
     */
    public static List<UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity> fromTransferOrderItemsInbound(
            List<TransferOrderItemEntity> items,
            Long unifiedOrderId,
            String sourceOrderNumber) {
        
        return items.stream()
            .map(item -> fromTransferOrderItemInbound(item, unifiedOrderId, sourceOrderNumber))
            .collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.toList());
    }
}

/**
 * 统一出库单转换类
 */
public final class UnifiedOutboundOrderConvert {
    
    /**
     * 从调拨单转换为统一出库单（源仓库）
     */
    public static UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity fromTransferOrderOutbound(
            TransferOrderEntity transferOrder,
            DocumentNumberService documentNumberService) {
        
        UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = new UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity();
        unifiedOrder.setOrderNumber(documentNumberService.generateUnifiedOutboundOrderNumber());
        unifiedOrder.setSourceDocumentType(BusinessTypeEnum.TRANSFER_OUT.getCode());
        unifiedOrder.setSourceDocumentId(transferOrder.getOrderNumber());
        unifiedOrder.setWarehouseId(transferOrder.getSourceWarehouseId());
        unifiedOrder.setBusinessDate(transferOrder.getBusinessDate());
        unifiedOrder.setStatus(OrderStatusEnum.COMPLETED.getCode());
        
        return unifiedOrder;
    }
    
    /**
     * 从销售出库单转换为统一出库单
     */
    public static UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity fromSalesOrder(
            SalesOrderEntity salesOrder,
            DocumentNumberService documentNumberService) {
        
        UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = new UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity();
        unifiedOrder.setOrderNumber(documentNumberService.generateUnifiedOutboundOrderNumber());
        unifiedOrder.setSourceDocumentType(BusinessTypeEnum.SALES_OUT.getCode());
        unifiedOrder.setSourceDocumentId(salesOrder.getOrderNumber());
        unifiedOrder.setWarehouseId(salesOrder.getWarehouseId());
        unifiedOrder.setBusinessDate(salesOrder.getOrderDate());
        unifiedOrder.setStatus(OrderStatusEnum.COMPLETED.getCode());
        
        return unifiedOrder;
    }
    
    /**
     * 从调拨单明细转换为统一出库单明细（源仓库）
     */
    public static UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity fromTransferOrderItemOutbound(
            TransferOrderItemEntity item,
            Long unifiedOrderId,
            String sourceOrderNumber) {
        
        UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity unifiedItem = new UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity();
        unifiedItem.setUnifiedOutboundOrderId(unifiedOrderId);
        unifiedItem.setProductId(item.getProductId());
        unifiedItem.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
        unifiedItem.setQuantity(item.getTransferQuantity());
        unifiedItem.setUnit(item.getUnit());
        unifiedItem.setBusinessType(BusinessTypeEnum.TRANSFER_OUT.getCode());
        unifiedItem.setRelatedDocumentType(DocumentTypeEnum.TR.getCode());
        unifiedItem.setRelatedDocumentId(sourceOrderNumber);
        
        return unifiedItem;
    }
    
    /**
     * 从销售订单明细转换为统一出库单明细
     */
    public static UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity fromSalesOrderItem(
            SalesOrderItemEntity item,
            Long unifiedOrderId,
            String sourceOrderNumber) {
        
        UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity unifiedItem = new UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity();
        unifiedItem.setUnifiedOutboundOrderId(unifiedOrderId);
        unifiedItem.setProductId(item.getProductId());
        unifiedItem.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
        unifiedItem.setQuantity(item.getQuantity());
        unifiedItem.setUnit(item.getUnit());
        unifiedItem.setBusinessType(BusinessTypeEnum.SALES_OUT.getCode());
        unifiedItem.setRelatedDocumentType(DocumentTypeEnum.ORD.getCode());
        unifiedItem.setRelatedDocumentId(sourceOrderNumber);
        
        return unifiedItem;
    }
    
    /**
     * 批量转换调拨单明细（出库）
     */
    public static List<UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity> fromTransferOrderItemsOutbound(
            List<TransferOrderItemEntity> items,
            Long unifiedOrderId,
            String sourceOrderNumber) {
        
        return items.stream()
            .map(item -> fromTransferOrderItemOutbound(item, unifiedOrderId, sourceOrderNumber))
            .collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.toList());
    }
    
    /**
     * 批量转换销售订单明细
     */
    public static List<UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity> fromSalesOrderItems(
            List<SalesOrderItemEntity> items,
            Long unifiedOrderId,
            String sourceOrderNumber) {
        
        return items.stream()
            .map(item -> fromSalesOrderItem(item, unifiedOrderId, sourceOrderNumber))
            .collect(java.util.stream.Collectors.toList());
    }
}
```

#### 5.1.2.3 业务单据验证类（Validation）

```java
/**
 * 采购入库单验证类
 */
public final class PurchaseInOrderValidation {
    
    /**
     * 验证审核入库单的前置条件
     */
    public static void validApproveInboundOrder(PurchaseInOrderEntity order) {
        if (order == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("采购入库单不存在");
        }
        
        if (!OrderStatusEnum.PENDING.getCode().equals(order.getStatus())) {
            throw new BusinessException("只有待审核状态的入库单才能审核");
        }
        
        if (order.getTargetWarehouseId() == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("目标仓库不能为空");
        }
        
        if (order.getBusinessDate() == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("业务日期不能为空");
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * 验证入库单明细
     */
    public static void validOrderItems(List<PurchaseInOrderItemEntity> items) {
        if (items == null || items.isEmpty()) {
            throw new BusinessException("入库单明细不能为空");
        }
        
        for (PurchaseInOrderItemEntity item : items) {
            if (item.getQuantity() == null || item.getQuantity() <= 0) {
                throw new BusinessException("入库数量必须大于0");
            }
            
            if (StringUtils.isBlank(item.getSkuCode())) {
                throw new BusinessException("SKU编码不能为空");
            }
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 调拨单验证类
 */
public final class TransferOrderValidation {
    
    /**
     * 验证创建调拨单的前置条件
     */
    public static void validCreate(AddTransferOrderRequest request) {
        if (request == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("调拨单请求不能为空");
        }
        
        if (request.getSourceWarehouseId() == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("源仓库不能为空");
        }
        
        if (request.getDestinationWarehouseId() == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("目标仓库不能为空");
        }
        
        if (request.getSourceWarehouseId().equals(request.getDestinationWarehouseId())) {
            throw new BusinessException("源仓库和目标仓库不能相同");
        }
        
        if (request.getItems() == null || request.getItems().isEmpty()) {
            throw new BusinessException("调拨单明细不能为空");
        }
        
        // 验证同一商品只能选择一个入库批次
        Map<String, Long> skuInboundOrderMap = new HashMap<>();
        for (AddTransferOrderItemRequest item : request.getItems()) {
            String key = item.getSkuCode() + "_" + item.getInboundOrderItemId();
            if (skuInboundOrderMap.containsKey(key)) {
                throw new BusinessException("同一商品在一次调拨中只能选择一个入库批次，SKU: " + item.getSkuCode());
            }
            skuInboundOrderMap.put(key, item.getInboundOrderItemId());
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * 验证提交调拨单时的可用库存
     */
    public static void validAvailableStock(List<TransferOrderItemEntity> items, 
                                          InboundOrderItemRepository inboundOrderItemRepository) {
        for (TransferOrderItemEntity item : items) {
            InboundOrderItemEntity inboundItem = inboundOrderItemRepository.selectById(
                item.getInboundOrderItemId()
            );
            
            if (inboundItem == null) {
                throw new BusinessException("入库单明细不存在，ID: " + item.getInboundOrderItemId());
            }
            
            // 可用库存 = 入库数量 - 已分配数量
            int availableQuantity = inboundItem.getInboundQuantity() - inboundItem.getAllocatedQuantity();
            
            if (availableQuantity < item.getTransferQuantity()) {
                throw new BusinessException(
                    String.format("可用库存不足，SKU: %s, 可用库存: %d, 调拨数量: %d",
                        item.getSkuCode(), availableQuantity, item.getTransferQuantity())
                );
            }
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * 验证审核出库的前置条件
     */
    public static void validApproveOutbound(TransferOrderEntity order) {
        if (order == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("调拨单不存在");
        }
        
        // 调拨单提交后状态保持为DRAFT，审核出库时检查DRAFT状态
        if (!OrderStatusEnum.DRAFT.getCode().equals(order.getStatus())) {
            throw new BusinessException("只有草稿状态的调拨单才能审核出库");
        }
        
        if (order.getSourceWarehouseId() == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("源仓库不能为空");
        }
        
        if (order.getDestinationWarehouseId() == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("目标仓库不能为空");
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * 验证审核入库的前置条件
     */
    public static void validApproveInbound(TransferOrderEntity order) {
        if (order == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("调拨单不存在");
        }
        
        if (!OrderStatusEnum.IN_TRANSIT.getCode().equals(order.getStatus())) {
            throw new BusinessException("只有运输中状态的调拨单才能审核入库");
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 销售出库单验证类
 */
public final class SalesOrderValidation {
    
    /**
     * 验证审核出库的前置条件
     */
    public static void validApproveOutbound(SalesOrderEntity order) {
        if (order == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("销售订单不存在");
        }
        
        if (!OrderStatusEnum.PENDING.getCode().equals(order.getStatus())) {
            throw new BusinessException("只有待审核状态的订单才能审核出库");
        }
        
        if (order.getWarehouseId() == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("仓库不能为空");
        }
    }
}
```

#### 5.1.2.4 采购入库单转换逻辑

```java
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class PurchaseInServiceImpl implements PurchaseInService {
    
    private final PurchaseInRepository purchaseInRepository;
    private final UnifiedOrderService unifiedOrderService;
    private final DocumentNumberService documentNumberService;
    
    /**
     * 审核通过采购入库单，转换为统一入库单并更新库存
     */
    @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
    @Override
    public void approveInboundOrder(Long inboundOrderId) {
        // 1. 查询并验证采购入库单
        PurchaseInOrderEntity inboundOrder = purchaseInRepository.selectById(inboundOrderId);
        PurchaseInOrderValidation.validApproveInboundOrder(inboundOrder);
        
        // 2. 查询并验证入库单明细
        List<PurchaseInOrderItemEntity> items = purchaseInRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(inboundOrderId);
        PurchaseInOrderValidation.validOrderItems(items);
        
        // 3. 转换为统一入库单
        UnifiedInboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = UnifiedInboundOrderConvert.fromPurchaseInOrder(
            inboundOrder, 
            documentNumberService
        );
        Long unifiedOrderId = unifiedOrderService.insertUnifiedInboundOrder(unifiedOrder);
        
        // 4. 转换为统一入库单明细
        List<UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity> unifiedItems = UnifiedInboundOrderConvert.fromPurchaseInOrderItems(
            items,
            unifiedOrderId,
            inboundOrder.getOrderNumber()
        );
        unifiedOrderService.batchInsertUnifiedInboundOrderItems(unifiedItems);
        
        // 5. 通过统一入库单更新库存（会记录库存流水）
        unifiedOrderService.increaseStockByUnifiedInbound(unifiedOrderId);
        
        // 6. 更新采购入库单状态
        updatePurchaseInOrderStatus(inboundOrder, OrderStatusEnum.INBOUNDED);
    }
    
    /**
     * 更新采购入库单状态
     */
    private void updatePurchaseInOrderStatus(PurchaseInOrderEntity order, OrderStatusEnum status) {
        order.setStatus(status.getCode());
        purchaseInRepository.updateById(order);
    }
}
```

#### 5.1.2.5 调拨单转换逻辑

```java
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class TransferOrderServiceImpl implements TransferOrderService {
    
    private final TransferOrderRepository transferOrderRepository;
    private final InboundOrderItemRepository inboundOrderItemRepository;
    private final UnifiedOrderService unifiedOrderService;
    private final DocumentNumberService documentNumberService;
    
    /**
     * 创建调拨单
     */
    @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
    @Override
    public Long createTransferOrder(AddTransferOrderRequest request) {
        // 1. 验证请求参数
        TransferOrderValidation.validCreate(request);
        
        // 2. 生成调拨单号
        String orderNumber = documentNumberService.generateTransferOrderNumber();
        
        // 3. 转换为调拨单实体
        TransferOrderEntity transferOrder = TransferOrderConvert.toEntity(request);
        transferOrder.setOrderNumber(orderNumber);
        transferOrder.setStatus(OrderStatusEnum.DRAFT.getCode());
        
        // 4. 保存调拨单
        Long transferOrderId = transferOrderRepository.insert(transferOrder);
        
        // 5. 保存调拨单明细
        List<TransferOrderItemEntity> items = TransferOrderConvert.toItemEntities(
            request.getItems(), 
            transferOrderId
        );
        transferOrderRepository.batchInsertItems(items);
        
        return transferOrderId;
    }
    
    /**
     * 提交调拨单（校验可用库存，但不更新库存）
     */
    @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
    @Override
    public void submitTransferOrder(Long transferOrderId) {
        // 1. 查询调拨单
        TransferOrderEntity transferOrder = transferOrderRepository.selectById(transferOrderId);
        if (transferOrder == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("调拨单不存在");
        }
        
        if (!OrderStatusEnum.DRAFT.getCode().equals(transferOrder.getStatus())) {
            throw new BusinessException("只有草稿状态的调拨单才能提交");
        }
        
        // 2. 查询调拨单明细
        List<TransferOrderItemEntity> items = transferOrderRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(transferOrderId);
        
        // 3. 验证可用库存（强制校验：可用库存 ≥ 调拨数量）
        TransferOrderValidation.validAvailableStock(items, inboundOrderItemRepository);
        
        // 4. 状态保持为DRAFT，不更新库存
        // 注意：提交后状态仍为DRAFT，等待审核出库时才更新库存
    }
    
    /**
     * 审核出库：转换为统一出库单
     */
    @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
    @Override
    public void approveOutbound(Long transferOrderId) {
        // 1. 查询并验证调拨单
        TransferOrderEntity transferOrder = transferOrderRepository.selectById(transferOrderId);
        TransferOrderValidation.validApproveOutbound(transferOrder);
        
        List<TransferOrderItemEntity> items = transferOrderRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(transferOrderId);
        
        // 2. 再次验证可用库存（双重校验）
        TransferOrderValidation.validAvailableStock(items, inboundOrderItemRepository);
        
        // 3. 转换为统一出库单（源仓库）
        UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity outboundOrder = UnifiedOutboundOrderConvert.fromTransferOrderOutbound(
            transferOrder,
            documentNumberService
        );
        Long outboundOrderId = unifiedOrderService.insertUnifiedOutboundOrder(outboundOrder);
        
        // 4. 转换为统一出库单明细
        List<UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity> outboundItems = UnifiedOutboundOrderConvert.fromTransferOrderItemsOutbound(
            items,
            outboundOrderId,
            transferOrder.getOrderNumber()
        );
        unifiedOrderService.batchInsertUnifiedOutboundOrderItems(outboundItems);
        
        // 5. 通过统一出库单扣减源仓库库存
        unifiedOrderService.decreaseStockByUnifiedOutbound(outboundOrderId);
        
        // 6. 更新调拨单状态为"运输中"
        updateTransferOrderStatus(transferOrder, OrderStatusEnum.IN_TRANSIT);
    }
    
    /**
     * 审核入库：转换为统一入库单
     */
    @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
    @Override
    public void approveInbound(Long transferOrderId) {
        // 1. 查询并验证调拨单
        TransferOrderEntity transferOrder = transferOrderRepository.selectById(transferOrderId);
        TransferOrderValidation.validApproveInbound(transferOrder);
        
        List<TransferOrderItemEntity> items = transferOrderRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(transferOrderId);
        
        // 2. 转换为统一入库单（目标仓库）
        UnifiedInboundOrderEntity inboundOrder = UnifiedInboundOrderConvert.fromTransferOrderInbound(
            transferOrder,
            documentNumberService
        );
        Long inboundOrderId = unifiedOrderService.insertUnifiedInboundOrder(inboundOrder);
        
        // 3. 转换为统一入库单明细
        List<UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity> inboundItems = UnifiedInboundOrderConvert.fromTransferOrderItemsInbound(
            items,
            inboundOrderId,
            transferOrder.getOrderNumber()
        );
        unifiedOrderService.batchInsertUnifiedInboundOrderItems(inboundItems);
        
        // 4. 通过统一入库单增加目标仓库库存
        unifiedOrderService.increaseStockByUnifiedInbound(inboundOrderId);
        
        // 5. 更新调拨单状态为"已完成"
        updateTransferOrderStatus(transferOrder, OrderStatusEnum.COMPLETED);
    }
    
    /**
     * 更新调拨单状态
     */
    private void updateTransferOrderStatus(TransferOrderEntity order, OrderStatusEnum status) {
        order.setStatus(status.getCode());
        transferOrderRepository.updateById(order);
    }
}
```

#### 5.1.2.6 销售出库单转换逻辑

> **重要更新**：销售出库单的完整实现逻辑（包含FIFO批次扣减）已移至 [5.4 批次库存FIFO扣减逻辑](#54-批次库存fifo扣减逻辑) 章节，请参考该章节获取完整实现代码。

**核心要点**：
- 销售出库单需要按照FIFO原则扣减批次库存
- 扣减时需要记录每个入库单的扣减明细
- 批次流水日志需要包含入库单级别的详细信息

**简化版实现示例**（完整实现请参考5.4章节）：

```java
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class SalesOutboundServiceImpl implements SalesOutboundService {
    
    private final SalesOutboundRepository salesOutboundRepository;
    private final BatchRepository batchRepository;
    private final UnifiedOrderService unifiedOrderService;
    
    /**
     * 审核出库：转换为统一出库单，并按照FIFO原则扣减批次库存
     * 
     * 完整实现请参考：5.4.3 FIFO扣减实现逻辑
     */
    @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
    @Override
    public void approveOutbound(Long salesOrderId) {
        // 1. 查询并验证销售订单
        SalesOrderEntity salesOrder = salesOutboundRepository.selectById(salesOrderId);
        SalesOrderValidation.validApproveOutbound(salesOrder);
        
        List<SalesOrderItemEntity> items = salesOutboundRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(salesOrderId);
        
        // 2. 转换为统一出库单
        UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity outboundOrder = UnifiedOutboundOrderConvert.fromSalesOrder(
            salesOrder,
            documentNumberService
        );
        Long outboundOrderId = unifiedOrderService.insertUnifiedOutboundOrder(outboundOrder);
        
        // 3. 按FIFO原则扣减批次库存并转换为统一出库单明细
        List<BatchDeductionDetail> batchDeductionDetails = processSalesOrderItems(
            items,
            salesOrder,
            outboundOrderId
        );
        
        // 4. 通过统一出库单扣减总库存
        unifiedOrderService.decreaseStockByUnifiedOutbound(outboundOrderId);
        
        // 5. 记录批次扣减流水（包含入库单明细，详见5.5）
        recordBatchDeductionItemLog(salesOrder.getOrderNumber(), batchDeductionDetails);
        
        // 6. 更新销售订单状态
        updateSalesOrderStatus(salesOrder, OrderStatusEnum.SHIPPED);
    }
    
    /**
     * 处理销售订单明细（按FIFO扣减批次库存并转换为统一出库单明细）
     */
    private List<BatchDeductionDetail> processSalesOrderItems(
            List<SalesOrderItemEntity> items,
            SalesOrderEntity salesOrder,
            Long outboundOrderId) {
        
        List<BatchDeductionDetail> batchDeductionDetails = new ArrayList<>();
        List<UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity> outboundItems = new ArrayList<>();
        
        for (SalesOrderItemEntity item : items) {
            // 按FIFO扣减批次库存
            List<BatchDeductionDetail> deductions = deductBatchStockByFIFO(
                item.getSkuCode(),
                salesOrder.getWarehouseId(),
                item.getQuantity()
            );
            batchDeductionDetails.addAll(deductions);
            
            // 转换为统一出库单明细
            UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity outboundItem = UnifiedOutboundOrderConvert.fromSalesOrderItem(
                item,
                outboundOrderId,
                salesOrder.getOrderNumber()
            );
            outboundItems.add(outboundItem);
        }
        
        unifiedOrderService.batchInsertUnifiedOutboundOrderItems(outboundItems);
        
        return batchDeductionDetails;
    }
    
    /**
     * 更新销售订单状态
     */
    private void updateSalesOrderStatus(SalesOrderEntity order, OrderStatusEnum status) {
        order.setStatus(status.getCode());
        salesOutboundRepository.updateById(order);
    }
    
    // deductBatchStockByFIFO 和 recordBatchDeductionItemLog 方法
    // 的完整实现请参考 5.4.3 和 5.5 章节
}
```

#### 5.1.3 统一库存更新服务核心实现

#### 5.1.3.1 库存流水日志转换类

```java
/**
 * 库存流水日志转换类
 */
public final class InventoryItemLogConvert {
    
    /**
     * 从统一入库单明细转换为库存流水日志
     */
    public static InventoryItemEntity fromUnifiedInboundItem(
            UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity item,
            UnifiedInboundOrderEntity order,
            InventoryEntity updatedInventory,
            Long warehouseId,
            String warehouseName,
            Long operatorId,
            String operatorName) {
        
        InventoryItemEntity itemLog = new InventoryItemEntity();
        itemLog.setProductId(item.getProductId());
        itemLog.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
        itemLog.setWarehouseId(warehouseId);
        itemLog.setWarehouseName(warehouseName);
        itemLog.setProductStatus(ProductStatusEnum.NORMAL.getCode());
        itemLog.setChangeTime(LocalDateTime.now());
        itemLog.setBusinessType(item.getBusinessType());
        itemLog.setRelatedDocumentType(item.getRelatedDocumentType());
        itemLog.setRelatedDocumentId(item.getRelatedDocumentId());
        itemLog.setChangeQuantity(item.getQuantity()); // 正数
        itemLog.setTotalBalanceAfterChange(updatedInventory.getTotalStock());
        itemLog.setOperatorId(operatorId);
        itemLog.setOperatorName(operatorName);

        return itemLog;
    }
    
    /**
     * 从统一出库单明细转换为库存流水日志
     */
    public static InventoryItemEntity fromUnifiedOutboundItem(
            UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity item,
            UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity order,
            InventoryEntity updatedInventory,
            Long warehouseId,
            String warehouseName,
            Long operatorId,
            String operatorName) {
        
        InventoryItemEntity itemLog = new InventoryItemEntity();
        itemLog.setProductId(item.getProductId());
        itemLog.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
        itemLog.setWarehouseId(warehouseId);
        itemLog.setWarehouseName(warehouseName);
        itemLog.setProductStatus(ProductStatusEnum.NORMAL.getCode());
        itemLog.setChangeTime(LocalDateTime.now());
        itemLog.setBusinessType(item.getBusinessType());
        itemLog.setRelatedDocumentType(item.getRelatedDocumentType());
        itemLog.setRelatedDocumentId(item.getRelatedDocumentId());
        itemLog.setChangeQuantity(-item.getQuantity()); // 负数表示减少
        itemLog.setTotalBalanceAfterChange(updatedInventory.getTotalStock());
        itemLog.setOperatorId(operatorId);
        itemLog.setOperatorName(operatorName);

        return itemLog;
    }
}
```

#### 5.1.3.2 库存更新辅助类

```java
/**
 * 库存更新辅助类
 * 封装库存查询、更新、流水记录等通用逻辑
 */
@Component
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class InventoryUpdateHelper {
    
    private final InventoryRepository inventoryRepository;
    private final InventoryItemRepository inventoryItemRepository;
    
    /**
     * 增加库存并记录流水
     */
    public void increaseStockWithItemLog(
            UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity item,
            Long warehouseId,
            String warehouseName,
            Long operatorId,
            String operatorName) {
        
        // 1. 查询或创建库存
        InventoryEntity inventory = getOrCreateInventory(item.getSkuCode(), warehouseId);
        
        // 2. 更新库存（带乐观锁）
        updateStockWithOptimisticLock(inventory, item.getQuantity());
        
        // 3. 重新查询更新后的库存
        InventoryEntity updatedInventory = getInventory(item.getSkuCode(), warehouseId);
        
        // 4. 记录库存流水
        UnifiedInboundOrderEntity dummyOrder = new UnifiedInboundOrderEntity();
        dummyOrder.setWarehouseId(warehouseId);
        InventoryItemEntity itemLog = InventoryItemLogConvert.fromUnifiedInboundItem(
            item,
            dummyOrder,
            updatedInventory,
            warehouseId,
            warehouseName,
            operatorId,
            operatorName
        );
        inventoryItemRepository.insert(itemLog);
    }
    
    /**
     * 减少库存并记录流水
     */
    public void decreaseStockWithItemLog(
            UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity item,
            Long warehouseId,
            String warehouseName,
            Long operatorId,
            String operatorName) {
        
        // 1. 查询库存并验证
        InventoryEntity inventory = getInventory(item.getSkuCode(), warehouseId);
        validateSufficientStock(inventory, item.getQuantity());
        
        // 2. 更新库存（带乐观锁）
        updateStockWithOptimisticLock(inventory, -item.getQuantity());
        
        // 3. 重新查询更新后的库存
        InventoryEntity updatedInventory = getInventory(item.getSkuCode(), warehouseId);
        
        // 4. 记录库存流水
        UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity dummyOrder = new UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity();
        dummyOrder.setWarehouseId(warehouseId);
        InventoryItemEntity itemLog = InventoryItemLogConvert.fromUnifiedOutboundItem(
            item,
            dummyOrder,
            updatedInventory,
            warehouseId,
            warehouseName,
            operatorId,
            operatorName
        );
        inventoryItemRepository.insert(itemLog);
    }
    
    /**
     * 获取或创建库存
     */
    private InventoryEntity getOrCreateInventory(String skuCode, Long warehouseId) {
        InventoryQueryRequest queryRequest = buildInventoryQueryRequest(skuCode, warehouseId);
        InventoryEntity inventory = inventoryRepository.selectBySkuAndWarehouse(queryRequest);
        
        if (inventory == null) {
            inventory = createNewInventory(skuCode, warehouseId);
        }
        
        return inventory;
    }
    
    /**
     * 获取库存
     */
    private InventoryEntity getInventory(String skuCode, Long warehouseId) {
        InventoryQueryRequest queryRequest = buildInventoryQueryRequest(skuCode, warehouseId);
        InventoryEntity inventory = inventoryRepository.selectBySkuAndWarehouse(queryRequest);
        
        if (inventory == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("库存记录不存在");
        }
        
        return inventory;
    }
    
    /**
     * 构建库存查询请求
     */
    private InventoryQueryRequest buildInventoryQueryRequest(String skuCode, Long warehouseId) {
        InventoryQueryRequest queryRequest = new InventoryQueryRequest();
        queryRequest.setSkuCode(skuCode);
        queryRequest.setWarehouseId(warehouseId);
        queryRequest.setProductStatus(ProductStatusEnum.NORMAL.getCode());
        return queryRequest;
    }
    
    /**
     * 创建新库存记录
     */
    private InventoryEntity createNewInventory(String skuCode, Long warehouseId) {
        InventoryEntity inventory = new InventoryEntity();
        inventory.setSkuCode(skuCode);
        inventory.setWarehouseId(warehouseId);
        inventory.setProductStatus(ProductStatusEnum.NORMAL.getCode());
        inventory.setTotalStock(0);
        inventory.setAllocatableStock(0);
        inventory.setAllocatedStock(0);
        inventory.setVersion(0);
        inventoryRepository.insert(inventory);
        return inventory;
    }
    
    /**
     * 验证库存充足
     */
    private void validateSufficientStock(InventoryEntity inventory, Integer quantity) {
        if (inventory == null || inventory.getTotalStock() < quantity) {
            throw new InsufficientStockException("库存不足");
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * 使用乐观锁更新库存
     */
    private void updateStockWithOptimisticLock(InventoryEntity inventory, Integer changeQuantity) {
        InventoryEntity updateEntity = new InventoryEntity();
        updateEntity.setSkuCode(inventory.getSkuCode());
        updateEntity.setWarehouseId(inventory.getWarehouseId());
        updateEntity.setProductStatus(inventory.getProductStatus());
        updateEntity.setVersion(inventory.getVersion());
        updateEntity.setChangeQuantity(changeQuantity);
        
        int updateCount = inventoryRepository.updateStockWithVersion(updateEntity);
        if (updateCount == 0) {
            throw new ConcurrentModificationException("库存更新失败，请重试");
        }
    }
}
```

#### 5.1.3.3 统一库存更新服务实现

```java
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class UnifiedOrderServiceImpl implements UnifiedOrderService {
    
    private final UnifiedInboundOrderRepository unifiedInboundOrderRepository;
    private final UnifiedOutboundOrderRepository unifiedOutboundOrderRepository;
    private final InventoryUpdateHelper inventoryUpdateHelper;
    
    /**
     * 通过统一入库单增加库存
     * 核心逻辑：更新库存表 + 记录库存流水（包含原始业务类型）
     */
    @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
    @Override
    public void increaseStockByUnifiedInbound(Long unifiedInboundOrderId) {
        // 1. 查询统一入库单
        UnifiedInboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = unifiedInboundOrderRepository.selectById(unifiedInboundOrderId);
        UnifiedOrderValidation.validUnifiedInboundOrder(unifiedOrder);
        
        // 2. 查询统一入库单明细（包含业务类型和原始单据信息）
        List<UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity> items = unifiedInboundOrderRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(unifiedInboundOrderId);
        
        // 3. 对每个明细项更新库存并记录流水
        String warehouseName = getWarehouseName(unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId());
        Long operatorId = getCurrentUserId();
        String operatorName = getCurrentUserName();
        
        for (UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity item : items) {
            inventoryUpdateHelper.increaseStockWithItemLog(
                item,
                unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId(),
                warehouseName,
                operatorId,
                operatorName
            );
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * 通过统一出库单减少库存
     * 核心逻辑：更新库存表 + 记录库存流水（包含原始业务类型）
     */
    @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
    @Override
    public void decreaseStockByUnifiedOutbound(Long unifiedOutboundOrderId) {
        // 1. 查询统一出库单
        UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = unifiedOutboundOrderRepository.selectById(unifiedOutboundOrderId);
        UnifiedOrderValidation.validUnifiedOutboundOrder(unifiedOrder);
        
        // 2. 查询统一出库单明细（包含业务类型和原始单据信息）
        List<UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity> items = unifiedOutboundOrderRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(unifiedOutboundOrderId);
        
        // 3. 对每个明细项更新库存并记录流水
        String warehouseName = getWarehouseName(unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId());
        Long operatorId = getCurrentUserId();
        String operatorName = getCurrentUserName();
        
        for (UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity item : items) {
            inventoryUpdateHelper.decreaseStockWithItemLog(
                item,
                unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId(),
                warehouseName,
                operatorId,
                operatorName
            );
        }
    }
    
    private String getWarehouseName(Long warehouseId) {
        // 实现获取仓库名称的逻辑
        return "";
    }
    
    private Long getCurrentUserId() {
        // 实现获取当前用户ID的逻辑
        return 0L;
    }
    
    private String getCurrentUserName() {
        // 实现获取当前用户名的逻辑
        return "";
    }
}

/**
 * 统一单验证类
 */
public final class UnifiedOrderValidation {
    
    public static void validUnifiedInboundOrder(UnifiedInboundOrderEntity order) {
        if (order == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("统一入库单不存在");
        }
    }
    
    public static void validUnifiedOutboundOrder(UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity order) {
        if (order == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("统一出库单不存在");
        }
    }
}
```

#### 5.1.4 批次库存FIFO扣减逻辑

#### 5.1.4.1 设计说明

**核心需求**：销售出库单扣减批次库存时，必须按照采购入库单的先后顺序（FIFO - First In First Out）进行扣减。

**业务场景**：
- 批次库存由多个采购入库单的库存组成
- 销售出库时需要按照入库时间顺序扣减
- 先扣最早入库的库存，不够再扣下一个

**示例**：
```
批次 BATCH-001 包含：
- IN-2023102401（2023-10-24入库）：1200个，当前可分配800个
- IN-2023102502（2023-10-25入库）：800个，当前可分配600个
- IN-2023110101（2023-11-01入库）：2000个，当前可分配2000个

销售出库单需要扣减1000个：
1. 先扣 IN-2023102401：扣减800个（全部扣完）
2. 再扣 IN-2023102502：扣减200个（剩余400个）
3. IN-2023110101：不扣减
```

#### 5.1.4.2 数据库设计支持

批次入库明细表 `bill_batch_detail` 已包含以下关键字段：
- `inbound_order_id`：入库单ID
- `inbound_order_number`：入库单号
- `inbound_date`：入库日期（用于排序）
- `initial_allocated_quantity`：初始分配数量
- `current_available_quantity`：当前可用数量

#### 5.1.4.3 FIFO扣减实现逻辑

```java
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class SalesOutboundServiceImpl implements SalesOutboundService {
    
    private final SalesOutboundRepository salesOutboundRepository;
    private final BatchRepository batchRepository;
    private final UnifiedOrderService unifiedOrderService;
    
    /**
     * 审核出库：转换为统一出库单，并按照FIFO原则扣减批次库存
     */
    @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
    @Override
    public void approveOutbound(Long salesOrderId) {
        SalesOrderEntity salesOrder = salesOutboundRepository.selectById(salesOrderId);
        List<SalesOrderItemEntity> items = salesOutboundRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(salesOrderId);
        
        // 创建统一出库单
        UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity outboundOrder = new UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity();
        outboundOrder.setOrderNumber(generateUnifiedOutboundOrderNumber());
        outboundOrder.setSourceDocumentType("SALES_OUT");
        outboundOrder.setSourceDocumentId(salesOrder.getOrderNumber());
        outboundOrder.setWarehouseId(salesOrder.getWarehouseId());
        outboundOrder.setBusinessDate(salesOrder.getOrderDate());
        outboundOrder.setStatus(OrderStatusEnum.COMPLETED.getCode());
        Long outboundOrderId = unifiedOrderService.insertUnifiedOutboundOrder(outboundOrder);
        
        // 创建统一出库单明细（按FIFO原则扣减批次库存）
        List<UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity> outboundItems = new ArrayList<>();
        List<BatchDeductionDetail> batchDeductionDetails = new ArrayList<>(); // 记录批次扣减明细
        
        for (SalesOrderItemEntity item : items) {
            // 按FIFO原则扣减批次库存
            List<BatchDeductionDetail> deductions = deductBatchStockByFIFO(
                item.getSkuCode(),
                salesOrder.getWarehouseId(),
                item.getQuantity()
            );
            
            // 记录批次扣减明细（用于后续记录批次流水）
            batchDeductionDetails.addAll(deductions);
            
            // 创建统一出库单明细
            UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity outboundItem = new UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity();
            outboundItem.setUnifiedOutboundOrderId(outboundOrderId);
            outboundItem.setProductId(item.getProductId());
            outboundItem.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
            outboundItem.setQuantity(item.getQuantity());
            outboundItem.setUnit(item.getUnit());
            outboundItem.setBusinessType("SALES_OUT");
            outboundItem.setRelatedDocumentType("ORD");
            outboundItem.setRelatedDocumentId(salesOrder.getOrderNumber());
            outboundItems.add(outboundItem);
        }
        
        unifiedOrderService.batchInsertUnifiedOutboundOrderItems(outboundItems);
        
        // 通过统一出库单扣减库存
        unifiedOrderService.decreaseStockByUnifiedOutbound(outboundOrderId);
        
        // 记录批次扣减流水（关键：记录每个入库单的扣减明细）
        recordBatchDeductionItemLog(salesOrder.getOrderNumber(), batchDeductionDetails);
        
        // 更新销售订单状态
        salesOrder.setStatus(OrderStatusEnum.SHIPPED.getCode());
        salesOutboundRepository.updateById(salesOrder);
    }
    
    /**
     * 按FIFO原则扣减批次库存
     * @param skuCode SKU编码
     * @param warehouseId 仓库ID
     * @param quantity 需要扣减的数量
     * @return 批次扣减明细列表
     */
    private List<BatchDeductionDetail> deductBatchStockByFIFO(
            String skuCode, Long warehouseId, Integer quantity) {
        
        // 1. 查询该SKU在该仓库的所有批次及其入库明细（按入库日期排序）
        List<BatchInboundDetailEntity> inboundDetails = batchRepository
            .selectAvailableInboundDetailsBySkuAndWarehouse(skuCode, warehouseId);
        
        // 按入库日期排序（FIFO：最早入库的在前）
        inboundDetails.sort(Comparator.comparing(BatchInboundDetailEntity::getInboundDate));
        
        List<BatchDeductionDetail> deductionDetails = new ArrayList<>();
        int remainingQuantity = quantity;
        
        // 2. 按顺序扣减每个入库单的库存
        for (BatchInboundDetailEntity detail : inboundDetails) {
            if (remainingQuantity <= 0) {
                break; // 已扣减完成
            }
            
            int availableQuantity = detail.getCurrentAvailableQuantity();
            if (availableQuantity <= 0) {
                continue; // 该入库单已无可用库存
            }
            
            // 计算本次扣减数量
            int deductQuantity = Math.min(remainingQuantity, availableQuantity);
            
            // 3. 更新批次入库明细的可用数量（带乐观锁）
            BatchInboundDetailEntity updateEntity = new BatchInboundDetailEntity();
            updateEntity.setId(detail.getId());
            updateEntity.setVersion(detail.getVersion());
            updateEntity.setChangeQuantity(-deductQuantity); // 负数表示减少
            
            int updateCount = batchRepository.updateInboundDetailQuantityWithVersion(updateEntity);
            if (updateCount == 0) {
                throw new ConcurrentModificationException("批次库存扣减失败，请重试");
            }
            
            // 4. 更新批次总库存
            BatchEntity batch = batchRepository.selectById(detail.getBatchId());
            BatchEntity batchUpdate = new BatchEntity();
            batchUpdate.setId(batch.getId());
            batchUpdate.setVersion(batch.getVersion());
            batchUpdate.setChangeQuantity(-deductQuantity);
            batchRepository.updateBatchQuantityWithVersion(batchUpdate);
            
            // 5. 记录扣减明细
            BatchDeductionDetail deductionDetail = new BatchDeductionDetail();
            deductionDetail.setBatchId(detail.getBatchId());
            deductionDetail.setBatchNumber(batch.getBatchNumber());
            deductionDetail.setInboundOrderId(detail.getInboundOrderId());
            deductionDetail.setInboundOrderNumber(detail.getInboundOrderNumber());
            deductionDetail.setInboundDate(detail.getInboundDate());
            deductionDetail.setDeductQuantity(deductQuantity);
            deductionDetail.setRemainingQuantity(availableQuantity - deductQuantity);
            deductionDetails.add(deductionDetail);
            
            remainingQuantity -= deductQuantity;
        }
        
        // 6. 检查是否扣减完成
        if (remainingQuantity > 0) {
            throw new InsufficientStockException(
                String.format("批次库存不足，还需要 %d 个", remainingQuantity)
            );
        }
        
        return deductionDetails;
    }
    
    /**
     * 记录批次扣减流水（记录每个入库单的扣减明细）
     */
    private void recordBatchDeductionItemLog(
            String salesOrderNumber, List<BatchDeductionDetail> deductionDetails) {
        
        for (BatchDeductionDetail detail : deductionDetails) {
            BatchItemLogEntity itemLog = new BatchItemLogEntity();
            itemLog.setBatchId(detail.getBatchId());
            itemLog.setBatchNumber(detail.getBatchNumber());
            itemLog.setChangeTime(LocalDateTime.now());
            itemLog.setBusinessAction("订单扣减"); // 业务动作：订单扣减
            itemLog.setRelatedDocumentType("ORD"); // 关联单据类型：订单
            itemLog.setRelatedDocumentId(salesOrderNumber); // 关联单据号：销售订单号
            itemLog.setChangeAmount(-detail.getDeductQuantity()); // 负数表示减少
            itemLog.setRemainingQuantity(detail.getRemainingQuantity()); // 扣减后的余量
            itemLog.setOperatorId(getCurrentUserId());
            itemLog.setOperatorName(getCurrentUserName());
            
            // 关键：记录入库单级别的明细信息（用于追溯）
            itemLog.setInboundOrderId(detail.getInboundOrderId());
            itemLog.setInboundOrderNumber(detail.getInboundOrderNumber());
            itemLog.setInboundDate(detail.getInboundDate());
            
            batchRepository.insertBatchItemLog(itemLog);
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 批次扣减明细（用于记录FIFO扣减的详细信息）
 */
@Data
class BatchDeductionDetail {
    private Long batchId;
    private String batchNumber;
    private Long inboundOrderId;
    private String inboundOrderNumber;
    private LocalDate inboundDate;
    private Integer deductQuantity;
    private Integer remainingQuantity;
}
```

#### 5.1.4.4 Repository层查询方法

```java
public interface BatchRepository {
    
    /**
     * 查询指定SKU和仓库的可用入库明细（按入库日期排序，用于FIFO扣减）
     */
    List<BatchInboundDetailEntity> selectAvailableInboundDetailsBySkuAndWarehouse(
        String skuCode, Long warehouseId
    );
    
    /**
     * 更新批次入库明细的可用数量（带乐观锁）
     */
    int updateInboundDetailQuantityWithVersion(BatchInboundDetailEntity entity);
    
    /**
     * 更新批次总库存（带乐观锁）
     */
    int updateBatchQuantityWithVersion(BatchEntity entity);
    
    /**
     * 插入批次流水日志
     */
    void insertBatchItemLog(BatchItemLogEntity itemLog);
}
```

#### 5.1.4.5 Mapper XML实现

```xml
<!-- 查询可用入库明细（按入库日期排序） -->
<select id="selectAvailableInboundDetailsBySkuAndWarehouse" resultType="BatchInboundDetailEntity">
    SELECT 
        bid.id,
        bid.batch_id,
        bid.inbound_order_id,
        bid.inbound_order_number,
        bid.inbound_date,
        bid.current_available_quantity,
        bid.version
    FROM bill_batch_detail bid
    INNER JOIN batch b ON bid.batch_id = b.id
    WHERE b.sku_id = #{skuId}
      AND b.warehouse_id = #{warehouseId}
      AND b.status = 'ON_SHELF'
      AND bid.current_available_quantity > 0
    ORDER BY bid.inbound_date ASC, bid.inbound_order_number ASC
</select>

<!-- 更新批次入库明细可用数量（带乐观锁） -->
<update id="updateInboundDetailQuantityWithVersion">
    UPDATE bill_batch_detail
    SET current_available_quantity = current_available_quantity + #{changeQuantity},
        version = version + 1
    WHERE id = #{id}
      AND version = #{version}
      AND current_available_quantity + #{changeQuantity} >= 0
</update>

<!-- 更新批次总库存（带乐观锁） -->
<update id="updateBatchQuantityWithVersion">
    UPDATE bill_inventory_batch
    SET total_quantity = total_quantity + #{changeQuantity},
        version = version + 1
    WHERE id = #{id}
      AND version = #{version}
</update>
```

### 5.5 批次流水明细说明

#### 5.1.5.1 批次流水明细的重要性

批次流水日志不仅记录批次级别的库存变动，还需要记录**入库单级别的明细信息**，以便：
1. **完整追溯**：可以追溯到具体是哪个采购入库单的库存被扣减
2. **FIFO验证**：可以验证是否按照入库顺序进行扣减
3. **问题排查**：当出现库存问题时，可以精确定位到具体的入库单

#### 5.1.5.2 批次明细表（流水）字段说明

`bill_inventory_batch_item` 表（与《数据库设计》2.2.7 一致）已包含用于 FIFO 追溯的字段：`bill_type`、`bill_id`、`bill_code`、`bill_item_id`、`bill_date`，无需再增加其他关联单据字段。建表语句以数据库设计文档 3.7 为准。

#### 5.1.5.3 批次流水明细展示

```java
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class BatchItemServiceImpl implements BatchItemService {
    
    private final BatchItemRepository batchItemRepository;
    
    /**
     * 查询批次流水日志（包含入库单明细信息）
     */
    @Override
    public IPage<BatchItemLogDTO> queryBatchItemLog(BatchItemLogQueryRequest request) {
        Page<BatchItemLogEntity> page = new Page<>(request.getPageIndex(), request.getPageSize());
        IPage<BatchItemLogEntity> entityPage = batchItemRepository.selectPage(page, request);
        
        // 转换为DTO，包含入库单明细信息
        IPage<BatchItemLogDTO> dtoPage = entityPage.convert(entity -> {
            BatchItemLogDTO dto = new BatchItemLogDTO();
            dto.setId(entity.getId());
            dto.setChangeTime(entity.getChangeTime());
            dto.setBusinessAction(getBusinessActionDisplayName(entity.getBusinessAction()));
            dto.setRelatedDocumentType(entity.getRelatedDocumentType());
            dto.setRelatedDocumentId(entity.getRelatedDocumentId());
            dto.setChangeAmount(entity.getChangeAmount());
            dto.setRemainingQuantity(entity.getRemainingQuantity());
            dto.setOperatorName(entity.getOperatorName());
            
            // 关键：展示入库单明细信息（如果是订单扣减）
            if ("订单扣减".equals(entity.getBusinessAction()) && entity.getInboundOrderNumber() != null) {
                dto.setInboundOrderNumber(entity.getInboundOrderNumber());
                dto.setInboundDate(entity.getInboundDate());
                dto.setDetailDescription(String.format(
                    "从入库单 %s（%s入库）扣减 %d 个，余量 %d 个",
                    entity.getInboundOrderNumber(),
                    entity.getInboundDate(),
                    Math.abs(entity.getChangeAmount()),
                    entity.getRemainingQuantity()
                ));
            }
            
            return dto;
        });
        
        return dtoPage;
    }
}
```

#### 5.1.5.4 批次流水明细展示示例

**前端展示格式**：

| 变动时间 | 业务动作 | 关联单据 | 入库单明细 | 变动量 | 余量 | 操作人 |
|---------|---------|---------|-----------|--------|------|--------|
| 2026-02-05 10:00:00 | 订单扣减 | ORD-20260205-001 | IN-2023102401（2023-10-24入库） | -800 | 0 | 系统 |
| 2026-02-05 10:00:00 | 订单扣减 | ORD-20260205-001 | IN-2023102502（2023-10-25入库） | -200 | 400 | 系统 |

**说明**：
- 一次销售出库可能产生多条批次流水记录（对应多个入库单）
- 每条记录都明确标注了是从哪个入库单扣减的
- 可以验证是否按照入库日期顺序进行扣减

#### 5.1.6 纳入新入库单资源功能

#### 5.1.6.1 功能说明

**业务需求**：在批次库存调整时，可以将新的采购入库单资源纳入到现有批次中。

**使用场景**：
1. 批次创建时遗漏了某些入库单
2. 新的采购入库单到货，需要纳入现有批次
3. 批次库存调整时，需要补充新的入库资源

#### 5.6.2 功能实现

```java
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class BatchServiceImpl implements BatchService {
    
    private final BatchRepository batchRepository;
    private final PurchaseInRepository purchaseInRepository;
    private final UnifiedOrderService unifiedOrderService;
    
    /**
     * 纳入新入库单资源到批次
     * @param batchId 批次ID
     * @param request 纳入请求（包含入库单明细ID和分配数量）
     */
    @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
    @Override
    public void includeNewInboundResources(Long batchId, IncludeInboundResourceRequest request) {
        // 1. 查询批次信息
        BatchEntity batch = batchRepository.selectById(batchId);
        if (batch == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("批次不存在");
        }
        if (!"ON_SHELF".equals(batch.getStatus())) {
            throw new BusinessException("只有上架状态的批次才能纳入新资源");
        }
        
        // 2. 验证商品和仓库一致性
        for (IncludeInboundResourceItem item : request.getItems()) {
            PurchaseInOrderItemEntity inboundItem = purchaseInRepository.selectItemById(item.getInboundOrderItemId());
            if (inboundItem == null) {
                throw new BusinessException("入库单明细不存在");
            }
            
            // 验证商品一致
            if (!batch.getProductId().equals(inboundItem.getProductId())) {
                throw new BusinessException("商品不一致，无法纳入");
            }
            
            // 验证仓库一致
            PurchaseInOrderEntity inboundOrder = purchaseInRepository.selectById(inboundItem.getInboundOrderId());
            if (!batch.getWarehouseId().equals(inboundOrder.getTargetWarehouseId())) {
                throw new BusinessException("仓库不一致，无法纳入");
            }
            
            // 验证可用数量
            if (inboundItem.getAvailableQuantity() < item.getAllocatedQuantity()) {
                throw new BusinessException(
                    String.format("入库单 %s 可用数量不足", inboundOrder.getOrderNumber())
                );
            }
        }
        
        // 3. 扣减入库单明细的可用数量（带乐观锁）
        int totalIncludedQuantity = 0;
        List<BatchInboundDetailEntity> newDetails = new ArrayList<>();
        
        for (IncludeInboundResourceItem item : request.getItems()) {
            PurchaseInOrderItemEntity inboundItem = purchaseInRepository.selectItemById(item.getInboundOrderItemId());
            PurchaseInOrderEntity inboundOrder = purchaseInRepository.selectById(inboundItem.getInboundOrderId());
            
            // 扣减入库单明细的可用数量
            PurchaseInOrderItemEntity updateEntity = new PurchaseInOrderItemEntity();
            updateEntity.setId(inboundItem.getId());
            updateEntity.setVersion(inboundItem.getVersion());
            updateEntity.setChangeAvailableQuantity(-item.getAllocatedQuantity());
            
            int updateCount = purchaseInRepository.updateAvailableQuantityWithVersion(updateEntity);
            if (updateCount == 0) {
                throw new ConcurrentModificationException("入库单资源扣减失败，请重试");
            }
            
            // 创建批次入库明细记录
            BatchInboundDetailEntity detail = new BatchInboundDetailEntity();
            detail.setBatchId(batchId);
            detail.setInboundOrderId(inboundOrder.getId());
            detail.setInboundOrderNumber(inboundOrder.getOrderNumber());
            detail.setInboundDate(inboundOrder.getBusinessDate());
            detail.setInitialAllocatedQuantity(item.getAllocatedQuantity());
            detail.setCurrentAvailableQuantity(item.getAllocatedQuantity());
            detail.setVersion(0);
            newDetails.add(detail);
            
            totalIncludedQuantity += item.getAllocatedQuantity();
        }
        
        // 4. 批量插入批次入库明细
        batchRepository.batchInsertInboundDetails(newDetails);
        
        // 5. 更新批次总库存（带乐观锁）
        BatchEntity batchUpdate = new BatchEntity();
        batchUpdate.setId(batchId);
        batchUpdate.setVersion(batch.getVersion());
        batchUpdate.setChangeQuantity(totalIncludedQuantity);
        
        int updateCount = batchRepository.updateBatchQuantityWithVersion(batchUpdate);
        if (updateCount == 0) {
            throw new ConcurrentModificationException("批次库存更新失败，请重试");
        }
        
        // 6. 记录批次流水日志
        BatchItemLogEntity itemLog = new BatchItemLogEntity();
        itemLog.setBatchId(batchId);
        itemLog.setBatchNumber(batch.getBatchNumber());
        itemLog.setChangeTime(LocalDateTime.now());
        itemLog.setBusinessAction("纳入新单据"); // 业务动作：纳入新单据
        itemLog.setRelatedDocumentType("BATCH_ADJUSTMENT"); // 关联单据类型：批次调整
        itemLog.setRelatedDocumentId(batch.getBatchNumber());
        itemLog.setChangeAmount(totalIncludedQuantity); // 正数表示增加
        itemLog.setRemainingQuantity(batch.getTotalQuantity() + totalIncludedQuantity);
        itemLog.setOperatorId(getCurrentUserId());
        itemLog.setOperatorName(getCurrentUserName());
        itemLog.setRemark(request.getReason()); // 纳入原因
        
        batchRepository.insertBatchItemLog(itemLog);
        
        // 7. 记录详细的入库单明细（可选：如果需要更详细的追溯）
        for (IncludeInboundResourceItem item : request.getItems()) {
            PurchaseInOrderItemEntity inboundItem = purchaseInRepository.selectItemById(item.getInboundOrderItemId());
            PurchaseInOrderEntity inboundOrder = purchaseInRepository.selectById(inboundItem.getInboundOrderId());
            
            // 可以记录更详细的流水，包含具体入库单信息
            BatchItemLogEntity detailItemLog = new BatchItemLogEntity();
            detailItemLog.setBatchId(batchId);
            detailItemLog.setBatchNumber(batch.getBatchNumber());
            detailItemLog.setChangeTime(LocalDateTime.now());
            detailItemLog.setBusinessAction("纳入新单据");
            detailItemLog.setRelatedDocumentType("IN");
            detailItemLog.setRelatedDocumentId(inboundOrder.getOrderNumber());
            detailItemLog.setInboundOrderId(inboundOrder.getId());
            detailItemLog.setInboundOrderNumber(inboundOrder.getOrderNumber());
            detailItemLog.setInboundDate(inboundOrder.getBusinessDate());
            detailItemLog.setChangeAmount(item.getAllocatedQuantity());
            detailItemLog.setRemainingQuantity(batch.getTotalQuantity() + totalIncludedQuantity);
            detailItemLog.setOperatorId(getCurrentUserId());
            detailItemLog.setOperatorName(getCurrentUserName());
            detailItemLog.setRemark(String.format("纳入入库单 %s，数量 %d", 
                inboundOrder.getOrderNumber(), item.getAllocatedQuantity()));
            
            batchRepository.insertBatchItemLog(detailItemLog);
        }
    }
}

/**
 * 纳入入库单资源请求
 */
@Data
class IncludeInboundResourceRequest {
    /**
     * 纳入的入库单明细列表
     */
    private List<IncludeInboundResourceItem> items;
    
    /**
     * 纳入原因
     */
    private String reason;
}

@Data
class IncludeInboundResourceItem {
    /**
     * 入库单明细ID
     */
    private Long inboundOrderItemId;
    
    /**
     * 分配数量
     */
    private Integer allocatedQuantity;
}
```

#### 5.6.3 查询可用入库单资源池

```java
/**
 * 查询批次可用的入库单资源池（用于纳入新资源）
 */
@Override
public IPage<AvailableInboundResourceDTO> queryAvailableInboundResources(
        AvailableInboundResourceQueryRequest request) {
    
    // 查询指定商品和仓库的可用入库单明细
    Page<PurchaseInOrderItemEntity> page = new Page<>(
        request.getPageIndex(), request.getPageSize()
    );
    
    IPage<PurchaseInOrderItemEntity> itemPage = purchaseInRepository
        .selectAvailableItemsByProductAndWarehouse(page, request);
    
    // 转换为DTO
    return itemPage.convert(item -> {
        PurchaseInOrderEntity order = purchaseInRepository.selectById(item.getInboundOrderId());
        
        AvailableInboundResourceDTO dto = new AvailableInboundResourceDTO();
        dto.setInboundOrderItemId(item.getId());
        dto.setInboundOrderId(order.getId());
        dto.setInboundOrderNumber(order.getOrderNumber());
        dto.setInboundDate(order.getBusinessDate());
        dto.setAvailableQuantity(item.getAvailableQuantity());
        dto.setUnit(item.getUnit());
        dto.setUnitCost(item.getUnitCost());
        dto.setExpiryDate(item.getExpiryDate());
        
        return dto;
    });
}
```

#### 5.1.7 库存流水查询和展示逻辑

```java
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class InventoryItemServiceImpl implements InventoryItemService {
    
    private final InventoryItemRepository inventoryItemRepository;
    
    /**
     * 查询库存流水日志
     * 对外展示时，显示原始业务类型（采购入库、销售出库、调拨入库、调拨出库等）
     */
    @Override
    public IPage<InventoryItemDTO> queryItemLog(InventoryItemQueryRequest request) {
        // 1. 构建查询条件
        InventoryItemQueryRequest queryRequest = new InventoryItemQueryRequest();
        queryRequest.setSkuCode(request.getSkuCode());
        queryRequest.setWarehouseId(request.getWarehouseId());
        queryRequest.setBusinessType(request.getBusinessType()); // 可以按业务类型筛选
        queryRequest.setRelatedDocumentId(request.getRelatedDocumentId()); // 可以按单据号搜索
        queryRequest.setStartDate(request.getStartDate());
        queryRequest.setEndDate(request.getEndDate());
        
        // 2. 分页查询
        Page<InventoryItemEntity> page = new Page<>(request.getPageIndex(), request.getPageSize());
        IPage<InventoryItemEntity> entityPage = inventoryItemRepository.selectPage(page, queryRequest);
        
        // 3. 转换为DTO（业务类型转换为中文显示）
        IPage<InventoryItemDTO> dtoPage = entityPage.convert(entity -> {
            InventoryItemDTO dto = new InventoryItemDTO();
            dto.setId(entity.getId());
            dto.setChangeTime(entity.getChangeTime());
            // 关键：使用原始业务类型，转换为中文显示
            dto.setBusinessType(getBusinessTypeDisplayName(entity.getBusinessType()));
            dto.setRelatedDocumentType(entity.getRelatedDocumentType());
            dto.setRelatedDocumentId(entity.getRelatedDocumentId()); // 显示原始单据号
            dto.setWarehouseName(entity.getWarehouseName());
            dto.setChangeQuantity(entity.getChangeQuantity());
            dto.setTotalBalanceAfterChange(entity.getTotalBalanceAfterChange());
            dto.setOperatorName(entity.getOperatorName());
            return dto;
        });
        
        return dtoPage;
    }
    
    /**
     * 业务类型转换为中文显示名称
     */
    private String getBusinessTypeDisplayName(String businessType) {
        switch (businessType) {
            case "PURCHASE_IN":
                return "采购入库";
            case "TRANSFER_IN":
                return "调拨入库";
            case "TRANSFER_OUT":
                return "调拨出库";
            case "SALES_OUT":
                return "销售出库";
            case "BATCH_ADJUSTMENT":
                return "批次调整";
            case "INVENTORY_ADJUSTMENT":
                return "库存盘点";
            default:
                return businessType;
        }
    }
}
```

#### 5.1.8 核心流程总结

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    subgraph Business["业务单据"]
        A[采购入库单]
        B[调拨单]
        C[销售出库单]
        D[批次调整]
    end
    
    subgraph Convert["转换"]
        E[统一入库/出库上下文<br/>代码层，不落统一表]
    end
    
    subgraph Context["上下文"]
        F[包含业务类型<br/>单据号、仓库、明细]
    end
    
    subgraph Inventory["库存"]
        G[更新 inventory<br/>写流水 bill_inventory_item]
    end
    
    subgraph Display["展示"]
        H[显示原始业务类型]
    end
    
    A & B & C & D --> E --> F --> G --> H
    
    style Business fill:#fff9c4
    style Convert fill:#e1f5ff
    style Context fill:#e8f5e9
    style Inventory fill:#c8e6c9
    style Display fill:#f3e5f5
```

#### 5.1.9 关键设计要点

1. **统一入库/出库上下文（代码层）必须包含业务追溯字段**
   - `business_type`: 记录原始业务类型（PURCHASE_IN, SALES_OUT 等）
   - `bill_type` / `bill_id` / `bill_code`: 记录单据类型与原始单据号，写流水时写入 `bill_inventory_item`

2. **库存流水写入 bill_inventory_item，从上下文中取业务信息**
   - 不记录"统一入库"或"统一出库"，而是记录原始业务类型（采购入库、销售出库、调拨入库、调拨出库等）
   - 数据库层无统一单据表，流水表即承载追溯信息

3. **对外展示时使用库存流水中的业务类型**
   - 前端查询库存流水时，显示原始业务类型
   - 用户看到的是"采购入库单增加了库存"，而不是"统一入库单增加了库存"

4. **追溯完整**
   - 通过 `bill_code`、`bill_id` 可追溯到原始业务单据
   - 通过 `business_type` 可区分不同业务场景

5. **扩展性**
   - 新增业务单据类型时，通过「上下文构建器 + 注册表」扩展，不修改统一库存服务（详见 5.2.5）

---

## 9. 数据库表结构

### 9.1 表结构设计原则

1. **统一字段规范**
   - 所有表包含：`id`(主键)、`create_time`、`update_time`
   - 需要并发控制的表包含：`version`(乐观锁版本号)
   - 软删除字段：`is_deleted`(0-未删除，1-已删除)

2. **索引设计**
   - 主键索引：`PRIMARY KEY (id)`
   - 唯一索引：业务唯一字段（如订单号、SKU编码）
   - 普通索引：外键字段、查询频繁字段

3. **字段类型规范**
   - 金额：`DECIMAL(18,2)`
   - 数量：`INT` 或 `BIGINT`
   - 日期：`DATE`
   - 时间：`DATETIME`
   - 版本号：`INT DEFAULT 0`

### 9.2 核心表结构

#### 4.2.1 商品表 (product)

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 | 约束 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| id | BIGINT | 主键ID | PK, AUTO_INCREMENT |
| sku_id | BIGINT | SKU ID | UK, NOT NULL |
| product_name | VARCHAR(255) | 商品名称 | NOT NULL |
| brand | VARCHAR(100) | 品牌 | |
| barcode | VARCHAR(100) | 条码 | |
| category | VARCHAR(100) | 分类 | |
| image_url | VARCHAR(500) | 商品图片URL | |
| unit | VARCHAR(20) | 单位 | |
| version | INT | 乐观锁版本号 | DEFAULT 0 |
| create_time | DATETIME | 创建时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP |
| update_time | DATETIME | 更新时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE |

#### 4.2.2 供应商表 (supplier)

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 | 约束 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| id | BIGINT | 主键ID | PK, AUTO_INCREMENT |
| supplier_code | VARCHAR(50) | 供应商编码 | UK, NOT NULL |
| supplier_name | VARCHAR(255) | 供应商名称 | NOT NULL |
| contact_person | VARCHAR(100) | 联系人 | |
| contact_phone | VARCHAR(50) | 联系电话 | |
| version | INT | 乐观锁版本号 | DEFAULT 0 |
| create_time | DATETIME | 创建时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP |
| update_time | DATETIME | 更新时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE |

#### 4.2.3 仓库表 (warehouse)

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 | 约束 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| id | BIGINT | 主键ID | PK, AUTO_INCREMENT |
| warehouse_code | VARCHAR(50) | 仓库编码 | UK, NOT NULL |
| warehouse_name | VARCHAR(255) | 仓库名称 | NOT NULL |
| warehouse_type | VARCHAR(50) | 仓库类型 | |
| address | VARCHAR(500) | 地址 | |
| version | INT | 乐观锁版本号 | DEFAULT 0 |
| create_time | DATETIME | 创建时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP |
| update_time | DATETIME | 更新时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE |

#### 4.2.4 采购入库单表 (inbound_order)

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 | 约束 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| id | BIGINT | 主键ID | PK, AUTO_INCREMENT |
| order_number | VARCHAR(50) | 入库单号 | UK, NOT NULL |
| supplier_id | BIGINT | 供应商ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| target_warehouse_id | BIGINT | 目标仓库ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| business_date | DATE | 业务日期 | NOT NULL |
| total_amount | DECIMAL(18,2) | 总金额 | DEFAULT 0 |
| status | VARCHAR(20) | 状态 | NOT NULL |
| remarks | VARCHAR(500) | 备注 | |
| creator_id | BIGINT | 创建人ID | |
| version | INT | 乐观锁版本号 | DEFAULT 0 |
| create_time | DATETIME | 创建时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP |
| update_time | DATETIME | 更新时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE |

**状态枚举值**：

| 状态码 | 状态名称 | 说明 |
|:------|:--------|:----|
| `DRAFT` | 📝 草稿 | 单据创建后的初始状态 |
| `PENDING` | ⏳ 待审核 | 单据已提交，等待审核 |
| `APPROVED` | ✅ 已审核 | 单据审核通过 |
| `INBOUNDED` | 📥 已入库 | 入库操作完成，库存已更新 |
| `CANCELLED` | ❌ 已取消 | 单据已取消 |

#### 4.2.5 采购入库单明细表 (inbound_order_item)

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 | 约束 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| id | BIGINT | 主键ID | PK, AUTO_INCREMENT |
| inbound_order_id | BIGINT | 入库单ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| product_id | BIGINT | 商品ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| sku_id | BIGINT | SKU ID | NOT NULL |
| quantity | INT | 入库数量 | NOT NULL |
| unit | VARCHAR(20) | 单位 | |
| unit_cost | DECIMAL(18,2) | 入库成本单价 | NOT NULL |
| expiry_date | DATE | 商品效期 | |
| subtotal | DECIMAL(18,2) | 小计 | NOT NULL |
| available_quantity | INT | 可用数量（池内可用） | DEFAULT 0 |
| version | INT | 乐观锁版本号 | DEFAULT 0 |
| create_time | DATETIME | 创建时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP |
| update_time | DATETIME | 更新时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE |

#### 4.2.6 调拨单表 (transfer_order)

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 | 约束 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| id | BIGINT | 主键ID | PK, AUTO_INCREMENT |
| order_number | VARCHAR(50) | 调拨单号 | UK, NOT NULL |
| source_warehouse_id | BIGINT | 调出仓库ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| destination_warehouse_id | BIGINT | 调入仓库ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| business_date | DATE | 业务日期 | NOT NULL |
| total_quantity | INT | 商品总数量 | DEFAULT 0 |
| status | VARCHAR(20) | 状态 | NOT NULL |
| remarks | VARCHAR(500) | 备注 | |
| creator_id | BIGINT | 创建人ID | |
| version | INT | 乐观锁版本号 | DEFAULT 0 |
| create_time | DATETIME | 创建时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP |
| update_time | DATETIME | 更新时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE |

**状态枚举值**：

| 状态码 | 状态名称 | 说明 |
|:------|:--------|:----|
| `DRAFT` | 📝 草稿 | 创建和提交后均为草稿状态，不更新库存 |
| `IN_TRANSIT` | 🚚 运输中 | 审核出库后，源仓库库存已扣减 |
| `COMPLETED` | ✅ 已完成 | 审核入库后，目标仓库库存已增加 |
| `CANCELLED` | ❌ 已取消 | 调拨单已取消 |

#### 4.2.7 调拨单明细表 (transfer_order_item)

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 | 约束 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| id | BIGINT | 主键ID | PK, AUTO_INCREMENT |
| transfer_order_id | BIGINT | 调拨单ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| inbound_order_item_id | BIGINT | 源入库单明细ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| product_id | BIGINT | 商品ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| sku_id | BIGINT | SKU ID | NOT NULL |
| transfer_quantity | INT | 调拨数量 | NOT NULL |
| unit | VARCHAR(20) | 单位 | |
| unit_cost | DECIMAL(18,2) | 单价成本（只读） | |
| expiry_date | DATE | 对应效期（只读） | |
| create_time | DATETIME | 创建时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP |
| update_time | DATETIME | 更新时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE |

#### 4.2.8 库存表 (inventory)

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 | 约束 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| id | BIGINT | 主键ID | PK, AUTO_INCREMENT |
| product_id | BIGINT | 商品ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| sku_id | BIGINT | SKU ID | NOT NULL |
| warehouse_id | BIGINT | 仓库ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| product_status | VARCHAR(50) | 产品状态（正品/次品） | NOT NULL, DEFAULT '正品' |
| total_stock | INT | 入库库存（总结余） | DEFAULT 0 |
| allocatable_stock | INT | 可分配库存 | DEFAULT 0 |
| allocated_stock | INT | 已分配合计 | DEFAULT 0 |
| locked_stock | INT | 锁定库存 | DEFAULT 0 |
| pending_shipment_stock | INT | 待发库存 | DEFAULT 0 |
| version | INT | 乐观锁版本号 | DEFAULT 0 |
| create_time | DATETIME | 创建时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP |
| update_time | DATETIME | 更新时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE |

**唯一约束**：`UNIQUE KEY uk_sku_warehouse_status (sku_id, warehouse_id, product_status)`

#### 4.2.9 库存流水表 (bill_inventory_item)

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 | 约束 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| id | BIGINT | 主键ID | PK, AUTO_INCREMENT |
| product_id | BIGINT | 商品ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| sku_id | BIGINT | SKU ID | NOT NULL |
| warehouse_id | BIGINT | 仓库ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| warehouse_name | VARCHAR(255) | 仓库名称（冗余） | |
| product_status | VARCHAR(50) | 产品状态 | NOT NULL |
| change_time | DATETIME | 变动时间 | NOT NULL |
| business_type | VARCHAR(50) | 业务类型 | NOT NULL |
| related_document_type | VARCHAR(50) | 关联单据类型 | NOT NULL |
| related_document_id | VARCHAR(100) | 关联单据号 | NOT NULL |
| change_quantity | INT | 变动数量 | NOT NULL |
| total_balance_after_change | INT | 变动后总结余 | NOT NULL |
| operator_id | BIGINT | 操作人ID | |
| operator_name | VARCHAR(100) | 操作人名称 | |
| create_time | DATETIME | 创建时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP |

**业务类型枚举值**：

| 业务类型码 | 业务类型名称 | 说明 |
|:----------|:-----------|:----|
| `PURCHASE_IN` | 📥 采购入库 | 采购商品入库操作 |
| `TRANSFER_IN` | 📥 调拨入库 | 调拨商品入库操作 |
| `TRANSFER_OUT` | 📤 调拨出库 | 调拨商品出库操作 |
| `SALES_OUT` | 📤 销售出库 | 销售商品出库操作 |
| `INVENTORY_ADJUSTMENT` | 🔧 库存盘点 | 库存盘点调整操作 |
| `ALLOCATE` | 🔒 分配 | 库存分配操作 |
| `DEALLOCATE` | 🔓 取消分配 | 取消库存分配操作 |

#### 4.2.10 批次表 (batch)

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 | 约束 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| id | BIGINT | 主键ID | PK, AUTO_INCREMENT |
| batch_number | VARCHAR(50) | 销售批次号 | UK, NOT NULL |
| product_id | BIGINT | 商品ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| sku_id | BIGINT | SKU ID | NOT NULL |
| warehouse_id | BIGINT | 仓库ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| storage_location | VARCHAR(50) | 库位 | |
| expiry_date | DATE | 到期日期 | |
| trade_mode | INT | 贸易模式（数据字典ID） | |
| customs_zone | INT | 申报关区（数据字典ID） | |
| status | INT | 状态（1-已上架，2-已下架） | NOT NULL |
| total_quantity | INT | 批次库存合计 | DEFAULT 0 |
| version | INT | 乐观锁版本号 | DEFAULT 0 |
| create_time | DATETIME | 创建时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP |
| update_time | DATETIME | 更新时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE |

**状态枚举值**：

| 状态码 | 状态名称 | 说明 |
|:------|:--------|:----|
| `ON_SHELF` | ✅ 已上架 | 批次发布即生效，无草稿状态 |
| `OFF_SHELF` | ❌ 已下架 | 批次作废，库存已返还到可用库存池 |

#### 4.2.11 批次单据明细表 (bill_batch_detail)

| 字段名 | 类型 | 说明 | 约束 |
|--------|------|------|------|
| id | BIGINT | 主键ID | PK, AUTO_INCREMENT |
| batch_id | INT | 批次ID | FK, NOT NULL |
| bill_item_id | INT | 单据明细ID（对应 bill_inventory_order_item.id） | FK, NOT NULL |
| bill_code | VARCHAR(50) | 单据号 | NOT NULL |
| bill_date | DATE | 单据日期 | |
| bill_status | INT | 单据状态 | NOT NULL |
| initial_allocated_quantity | DECIMAL(18,2) | 初始分配量 | NOT NULL |
| current_available_quantity | DECIMAL(18,2) | 当前可售余量 | NOT NULL |
| status | INT | 状态 | NOT NULL |
| version | INT | 乐观锁版本号 | DEFAULT 0 |
| create_time | DATETIME | 创建时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP |
| update_time | DATETIME | 更新时间 | DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE |

---

## 10. 创建SQL

### 9.1 商品表

```sql
CREATE TABLE `product` (
    `id` BIGINT(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '主键ID',
    `sku_id` BIGINT NOT NULL COMMENT 'SKU ID',
    `product_name` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL COMMENT '商品名称',
    `brand` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '品牌',
    `barcode` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '条码',
    `category` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '分类',
    `image_url` VARCHAR(500) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '商品图片URL',
    `unit` VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '单位',
    `version` INT(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '乐观锁版本号',
    `create_time` DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
    `update_time` DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
    PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
    UNIQUE KEY `uk_sku_id` (`sku_id`),
    KEY `idx_product_name` (`product_name`),
    KEY `idx_barcode` (`barcode`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COMMENT='商品表';
```

### 9.2 供应商表

```sql
CREATE TABLE `supplier` (
    `id` BIGINT(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '主键ID',
    `supplier_code` VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL COMMENT '供应商编码',
    `supplier_name` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL COMMENT '供应商名称',
    `contact_person` VARCHAR(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '联系人',
    `contact_phone` VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '联系电话',
    `version` INT(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '乐观锁版本号',
    `create_time` DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
    `update_time` DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
    PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
    UNIQUE KEY `uk_supplier_code` (`supplier_code`),
    KEY `idx_supplier_name` (`supplier_name`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COMMENT='供应商表';
```

### 9.3 仓库表

```sql
CREATE TABLE `warehouse` (
    `id` BIGINT(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '主键ID',
    `warehouse_code` VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL COMMENT '仓库编码',
    `warehouse_name` VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL COMMENT '仓库名称',
    `warehouse_type` VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '仓库类型',
    `address` VARCHAR(500) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '地址',
    `version` INT(11) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '乐观锁版本号',
    `create_time` DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
    `update_time` DATETIME NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
    PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
    UNIQUE KEY `uk_warehouse_code` (`warehouse_code`),
    KEY `idx_warehouse_name` (`warehouse_name`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COMMENT='仓库表';
```

### 9.4 采购入库单表

```sql
CREATE TABLE `inbound_order` (
    `id` BIGINT(20) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '主键ID',
    `order_number` VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL COMMENT '入库单号',
    `supplier_id` BIGINT(20) NOT NULL COMMENT '供应商ID',
    `target_warehouse_id` BIGINT(20) NOT NULL COMMENT '目标仓库ID',
    `business_date` DATE NOT NULL COMMENT '业务日期',
    `total_amount` DECIMAL(18,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '总金额',
    `status` VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL COMMENT '状态：DRAFT-草稿，PENDING-待审核，APPROVED-已审核，INBOUNDED-已入库，CANCELLED-已取消',
```
