## 12. 单元测试

### 12.1 测试策略

核心逻辑必须编写单元测试，确保：
1. **业务逻辑正确性**：验证库存更新逻辑的正确性
2. **并发安全性**：验证乐观锁机制的有效性
3. **异常处理**：验证各种异常场景的处理
4. **数据一致性**：验证库存流水记录的完整性

**详细测试用例**：详见 [库存管理系统测试用例](./测试用例.md)

### 12.2 统一库存更新服务单元测试

```java
@SpringBootTest
@Transactional
class UnifiedOrderServiceImplTest {
    
    @Autowired
    private UnifiedOrderService unifiedOrderService;
    
    @Autowired
    private UnifiedInboundOrderRepository unifiedInboundOrderRepository;
    
    @Autowired
    private InventoryRepository inventoryRepository;
    
    @Autowired
    private InventoryItemRepository inventoryItemRepository;
    
    /**
     * 测试：通过统一入库单增加库存
     * 验证：1. 库存数量正确增加 2. 库存流水记录原始业务类型
     */
    @Test
    void testIncreaseStockByUnifiedInbound() {
        // 1. 准备测试数据
        UnifiedInboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = createTestUnifiedInboundOrder();
        unifiedOrder.setSourceDocumentType("PURCHASE_IN");
        unifiedOrder.setSourceDocumentId("IN-2023102401");
        Long unifiedOrderId = unifiedInboundOrderRepository.insert(unifiedOrder);
        
        UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity item = createTestUnifiedInboundOrderItem(unifiedOrderId);
        item.setBusinessType("PURCHASE_IN"); // 原始业务类型
        item.setRelatedDocumentType("IN");
        item.setRelatedDocumentId("IN-2023102401");
        unifiedInboundOrderRepository.insertItem(item);
        
        // 2. 创建初始库存
        InventoryEntity initialInventory = createTestInventory();
        initialInventory.setTotalStock(100);
        initialInventory.setAllocatableStock(100);
        inventoryRepository.insert(initialInventory);
        
        // 3. 执行测试
        unifiedOrderService.increaseStockByUnifiedInbound(unifiedOrderId);
        
        // 4. 验证库存更新
        InventoryQueryRequest queryRequest = new InventoryQueryRequest();
        queryRequest.setSkuCode("SKU-IN001");
        queryRequest.setWarehouseId(1L);
        queryRequest.setProductStatus("正品");
        InventoryEntity updatedInventory = inventoryRepository.selectBySkuAndWarehouse(queryRequest);
        
        assertEquals(150, updatedInventory.getTotalStock()); // 100 + 50
        assertEquals(150, updatedInventory.getAllocatableStock());
        assertEquals(1, updatedInventory.getVersion()); // 版本号应该+1
        
        // 5. 验证库存流水记录（关键：验证记录的是原始业务类型）
        InventoryItemQueryRequest itemQuery = new InventoryItemQueryRequest();
        itemQuery.setSkuCode("SKU-IN001");
        itemQuery.setRelatedDocumentId("IN-2023102401");
        List<InventoryItemEntity> itemLogs = inventoryItemRepository.selectList(itemQuery);
        
        assertEquals(1, itemLogs.size());
        InventoryItemEntity itemLog = itemLogs.get(0);
        assertEquals("PURCHASE_IN", itemLog.getBusinessType()); // 验证是原始业务类型，不是"统一入库"
        assertEquals("IN", itemLog.getRelatedDocumentType());
        assertEquals("IN-2023102401", itemLog.getRelatedDocumentId());
        assertEquals(50, itemLog.getChangeQuantity()); // 正数表示增加
        assertEquals(150, itemLog.getTotalBalanceAfterChange());
    }
    
    /**
     * 测试：通过统一出库单减少库存
     * 验证：1. 库存数量正确减少 2. 库存流水记录原始业务类型
     */
    @Test
    void testDecreaseStockByUnifiedOutbound() {
        // 1. 准备测试数据
        UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = createTestUnifiedOutboundOrder();
        unifiedOrder.setSourceDocumentType("SALES_OUT");
        unifiedOrder.setSourceDocumentId("ORD-20231026-8891");
        Long unifiedOrderId = unifiedOutboundOrderRepository.insert(unifiedOrder);
        
        UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity item = createTestUnifiedOutboundOrderItem(unifiedOrderId);
        item.setBusinessType("SALES_OUT"); // 原始业务类型
        item.setRelatedDocumentType("ORD");
        item.setRelatedDocumentId("ORD-20231026-8891");
        unifiedOutboundOrderRepository.insertItem(item);
        
        // 2. 创建初始库存
        InventoryEntity initialInventory = createTestInventory();
        initialInventory.setTotalStock(100);
        initialInventory.setAllocatableStock(100);
        inventoryRepository.insert(initialInventory);
        
        // 3. 执行测试
        unifiedOrderService.decreaseStockByUnifiedOutbound(unifiedOrderId);
        
        // 4. 验证库存更新
        InventoryQueryRequest queryRequest = new InventoryQueryRequest();
        queryRequest.setSkuCode("SKU-IN001");
        queryRequest.setWarehouseId(1L);
        queryRequest.setProductStatus("正品");
        InventoryEntity updatedInventory = inventoryRepository.selectBySkuAndWarehouse(queryRequest);
        
        assertEquals(50, updatedInventory.getTotalStock()); // 100 - 50
        assertEquals(50, updatedInventory.getAllocatableStock());
        assertEquals(1, updatedInventory.getVersion());
        
        // 5. 验证库存流水记录（关键：验证记录的是原始业务类型）
        InventoryItemQueryRequest itemQuery = new InventoryItemQueryRequest();
        itemQuery.setSkuCode("SKU-IN001");
        itemQuery.setRelatedDocumentId("ORD-20231026-8891");
        List<InventoryItemEntity> itemLogs = inventoryItemRepository.selectList(itemQuery);
        
        assertEquals(1, itemLogs.size());
        InventoryItemEntity itemLog = itemLogs.get(0);
        assertEquals("SALES_OUT", itemLog.getBusinessType()); // 验证是原始业务类型，不是"统一出库"
        assertEquals("ORD", itemLog.getRelatedDocumentType());
        assertEquals("ORD-20231026-8891", itemLog.getRelatedDocumentId());
        assertEquals(-50, itemLog.getChangeQuantity()); // 负数表示减少
        assertEquals(50, itemLog.getTotalBalanceAfterChange());
    }
    
    /**
     * 测试：并发更新库存（乐观锁）
     * 验证：并发冲突时抛出异常或重试成功
     */
    @Test
    void testConcurrentUpdateStock() throws InterruptedException {
        // 1. 创建初始库存
        InventoryEntity initialInventory = createTestInventory();
        initialInventory.setTotalStock(100);
        initialInventory.setVersion(0);
        inventoryRepository.insert(initialInventory);
        
        // 2. 模拟并发更新
        CountDownLatch latch = new CountDownLatch(2);
        AtomicInteger successCount = new AtomicInteger(0);
        AtomicInteger failCount = new AtomicInteger(0);
        
        ExecutorService executor = Executors.newFixedThreadPool(2);
        
        // 线程1：更新库存
        executor.submit(() -> {
            try {
                InventoryEntity entity = new InventoryEntity();
                entity.setSkuCode("SKU-IN001");
                entity.setWarehouseId(1L);
                entity.setProductStatus("正品");
                entity.setVersion(0); // 都使用版本0
                entity.setChangeQuantity(10);
                
                int count = inventoryRepository.updateStockWithVersion(entity);
                if (count > 0) {
                    successCount.incrementAndGet();
                } else {
                    failCount.incrementAndGet();
                }
            } finally {
                latch.countDown();
            }
        });
        
        // 线程2：同时更新库存
        executor.submit(() -> {
            try {
                InventoryEntity entity = new InventoryEntity();
                entity.setSkuCode("SKU-IN001");
                entity.setWarehouseId(1L);
                entity.setProductStatus("正品");
                entity.setVersion(0); // 都使用版本0
                entity.setChangeQuantity(20);
                
                int count = inventoryRepository.updateStockWithVersion(entity);
                if (count > 0) {
                    successCount.incrementAndGet();
                } else {
                    failCount.incrementAndGet();
                }
            } finally {
                latch.countDown();
            }
        });
        
        // 3. 等待所有线程完成
        latch.await(5, TimeUnit.SECONDS);
        executor.shutdown();
        
        // 4. 验证：只有一个线程成功，另一个失败
        assertEquals(1, successCount.get());
        assertEquals(1, failCount.get());
        
        // 5. 验证最终库存（应该是100+10或100+20，只有一个生效）
        InventoryQueryRequest queryRequest = new InventoryQueryRequest();
        queryRequest.setSkuCode("SKU-IN001");
        queryRequest.setWarehouseId(1L);
        queryRequest.setProductStatus("正品");
        InventoryEntity finalInventory = inventoryRepository.selectBySkuAndWarehouse(queryRequest);
        
        assertTrue(finalInventory.getTotalStock() == 110 || finalInventory.getTotalStock() == 120);
        assertEquals(1, finalInventory.getVersion()); // 版本号应该+1
    }
    
    /**
     * 测试：库存不足时抛出异常
     */
    @Test
    void testInsufficientStock() {
        // 1. 创建初始库存（数量不足）
        InventoryEntity initialInventory = createTestInventory();
        initialInventory.setTotalStock(10);
        initialInventory.setAllocatableStock(10);
        inventoryRepository.insert(initialInventory);
        
        // 2. 创建统一出库单（出库数量大于库存）
        UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = createTestUnifiedOutboundOrder();
        Long unifiedOrderId = unifiedOutboundOrderRepository.insert(unifiedOrder);
        
        UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity item = createTestUnifiedOutboundOrderItem(unifiedOrderId);
        item.setQuantity(50); // 出库50，但库存只有10
        unifiedOutboundOrderRepository.insertItem(item);
        
        // 3. 执行测试，应该抛出异常
        assertThrows(InsufficientStockException.class, () -> {
            unifiedOrderService.decreaseStockByUnifiedOutbound(unifiedOrderId);
        });
        
        // 4. 验证库存未变化
        InventoryQueryRequest queryRequest = new InventoryQueryRequest();
        queryRequest.setSkuCode("SKU-IN001");
        queryRequest.setWarehouseId(1L);
        queryRequest.setProductStatus("正品");
        InventoryEntity inventory = inventoryRepository.selectBySkuAndWarehouse(queryRequest);
        
        assertEquals(10, inventory.getTotalStock()); // 库存未变化
    }
}
```

### 11.3 采购入库单转换逻辑单元测试

```java
@SpringBootTest
@Transactional
class PurchaseInServiceImplTest {
    
    @Autowired
    private PurchaseInService purchaseInService;
    
    @Autowired
    private PurchaseInRepository purchaseInRepository;
    
    @Autowired
    private UnifiedInboundOrderRepository unifiedInboundOrderRepository;
    
    @Autowired
    private InventoryItemRepository inventoryItemRepository;
    
    /**
     * 测试：审核通过采购入库单，转换为统一入库单并更新库存
     * 验证：1. 构建统一入库上下文并调用库存服务 2. 流水（bill_inventory_item）记录原始业务类型与单据号
     */
    @Test
    void testApproveInboundOrder() {
        // 1. 创建采购入库单
        PurchaseInOrderEntity inboundOrder = createTestPurchaseInOrder();
        inboundOrder.setOrderNumber("IN-2023102401");
        inboundOrder.setStatus("PENDING");
        Long inboundOrderId = purchaseInRepository.insert(inboundOrder);
        
        PurchaseInOrderItemEntity item = createTestPurchaseInOrderItem(inboundOrderId);
        item.setQuantity(100);
        purchaseInRepository.insertItem(item);
        
        // 2. 执行审核
        purchaseInService.approveInboundOrder(inboundOrderId);
        
        // 3. 验证采购入库单状态更新
        PurchaseInOrderEntity updatedOrder = purchaseInRepository.selectById(inboundOrderId);
        assertEquals("INBOUNDED", updatedOrder.getStatus());
        
        // 4. 验证创建了统一入库单
        UnifiedInboundOrderQueryRequest queryRequest = new UnifiedInboundOrderQueryRequest();
        queryRequest.setSourceDocumentId("IN-2023102401");
        List<UnifiedInboundOrderEntity> unifiedOrders = unifiedInboundOrderRepository.selectList(queryRequest);
        
        assertEquals(1, unifiedOrders.size());
        UnifiedInboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = unifiedOrders.get(0);
        assertEquals("PURCHASE_IN", unifiedOrder.getSourceDocumentType());
        assertEquals("IN-2023102401", unifiedOrder.getSourceDocumentId());
        
        // 5. 验证统一入库单明细保存了原始业务信息
        List<UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity> unifiedItems = unifiedInboundOrderRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(unifiedOrder.getId());
        assertEquals(1, unifiedItems.size());
        UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity unifiedItem = unifiedItems.get(0);
        assertEquals("PURCHASE_IN", unifiedItem.getBusinessType()); // 原始业务类型
        assertEquals("IN", unifiedItem.getRelatedDocumentType());
        assertEquals("IN-2023102401", unifiedItem.getRelatedDocumentId());
        
        // 6. 验证库存流水记录原始业务类型
        InventoryItemQueryRequest itemQuery = new InventoryItemQueryRequest();
        itemQuery.setRelatedDocumentId("IN-2023102401");
        List<InventoryItemEntity> itemLogs = inventoryItemRepository.selectList(itemQuery);
        
        assertEquals(1, itemLogs.size());
        InventoryItemEntity itemLog = itemLogs.get(0);
        assertEquals("PURCHASE_IN", itemLog.getBusinessType()); // 验证是"采购入库"，不是"统一入库"
        assertEquals("IN", itemLog.getRelatedDocumentType());
        assertEquals("IN-2023102401", itemLog.getRelatedDocumentId());
    }
}
```

### 12.4 调拨单转换逻辑单元测试

```java
@SpringBootTest
@Transactional
class TransferOrderServiceImplTest {
    
    @Autowired
    private TransferOrderService transferOrderService;
    
    @Autowired
    private TransferOrderRepository transferOrderRepository;
    
    @Autowired
    private UnifiedOutboundOrderRepository unifiedOutboundOrderRepository;
    
    @Autowired
    private UnifiedInboundOrderRepository unifiedInboundOrderRepository;
    
    /**
     * 测试：调拨单审核出库和确认入库
     * 验证：1. 审核出库构建统一出库上下文并调用库存服务（源仓库） 2. 确认入库构建统一入库上下文并调用库存服务（目标仓库）
     *       3. 库存流水分别记录调拨出库和调拨入库
     */
    @Test
    void testTransferOrderFlow() {
        // 1. 创建调拨单
        TransferOrderEntity transferOrder = createTestTransferOrder();
        transferOrder.setOrderNumber("TR-20231026001");
        transferOrder.setStatus(OrderStatusEnum.DRAFT.getCode());
        Long transferOrderId = transferOrderRepository.insert(transferOrder);
        
        TransferOrderItemEntity item = createTestTransferOrderItem(transferOrderId);
        item.setTransferQuantity(50);
        transferOrderRepository.insertItem(item);
        
        // 2. 创建源仓库和目标仓库的初始库存
        createTestInventory(1L, "SKU-IN001", 100); // 源仓库
        createTestInventory(2L, "SKU-IN001", 50);  // 目标仓库
        
        // 3. 执行审核出库
        transferOrderService.approveOutbound(transferOrderId);
        
        // 4. 验证创建了统一出库单（源仓库）
        UnifiedOutboundOrderQueryRequest outboundQuery = new UnifiedOutboundOrderQueryRequest();
        outboundQuery.setSourceDocumentId("TR-20231026001");
        List<UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity> outboundOrders = unifiedOutboundOrderRepository.selectList(outboundQuery);
        
        assertEquals(1, outboundOrders.size());
        UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity outboundOrder = outboundOrders.get(0);
        assertEquals("TRANSFER_OUT", outboundOrder.getSourceDocumentType());
        assertEquals(1L, outboundOrder.getWarehouseId()); // 源仓库
        
        // 验证统一出库单明细的业务类型
        List<UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity> outboundItems = unifiedOutboundOrderRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(outboundOrder.getId());
        assertEquals("TRANSFER_OUT", outboundItems.get(0).getBusinessType());
        
        // 5. 执行确认入库
        transferOrderService.confirmInbound(transferOrderId);
        
        // 6. 验证创建了统一入库单（目标仓库）
        UnifiedInboundOrderQueryRequest inboundQuery = new UnifiedInboundOrderQueryRequest();
        inboundQuery.setSourceDocumentId("TR-20231026001");
        List<UnifiedInboundOrderEntity> inboundOrders = unifiedInboundOrderRepository.selectList(inboundQuery);
        
        assertEquals(1, inboundOrders.size());
        UnifiedInboundOrderEntity inboundOrder = inboundOrders.get(0);
        assertEquals("TRANSFER_IN", inboundOrder.getSourceDocumentType());
        assertEquals(2L, inboundOrder.getWarehouseId()); // 目标仓库
        
        // 验证统一入库单明细的业务类型
        List<UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity> inboundItems = unifiedInboundOrderRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(inboundOrder.getId());
        assertEquals("TRANSFER_IN", inboundItems.get(0).getBusinessType());
        
        // 7. 验证库存流水记录
        InventoryItemQueryRequest itemQuery = new InventoryItemQueryRequest();
        itemQuery.setRelatedDocumentId("TR-20231026001");
        List<InventoryItemEntity> itemLogs = inventoryItemRepository.selectList(itemQuery);
        
        assertEquals(2, itemLogs.size()); // 应该有两条流水：一条出库，一条入库
        
        // 验证出库流水
        InventoryItemEntity outboundItem = itemLogs.stream()
            .filter(f -> "TRANSFER_OUT".equals(f.getBusinessType()))
            .findFirst()
            .orElseThrow();
        assertEquals(-50, outboundItem.getChangeQuantity());
        
        // 验证入库流水
        InventoryItemEntity inboundItem = itemLogs.stream()
            .filter(f -> "TRANSFER_IN".equals(f.getBusinessType()))
            .findFirst()
            .orElseThrow();
        assertEquals(50, inboundItem.getChangeQuantity());
    }
}
```

### 12.5 测试覆盖率要求

核心逻辑的单元测试覆盖率应达到：
- **统一库存更新服务**：覆盖率 ≥ 90%
- **业务单据转换逻辑**：覆盖率 ≥ 85%
- **库存流水记录逻辑**：覆盖率 ≥ 90%
- **并发控制逻辑**：覆盖率 ≥ 95%

---

### 9.2 关键实现要点

1. **事务管理**：所有写操作必须在 `BizService` 层使用 `@Transactional` 注解
2. **乐观锁**：所有库存更新操作必须使用 `version` 字段进行版本校验
3. **异常处理**：并发冲突时抛出 `ConcurrentModificationException`，由上层处理重试
4. **数据校验**：使用 `Validation` 类进行业务规则校验
5. **对象转换**：使用 `Convert` 类进行 Request、Entity、DTO 之间的转换
6. **统一库存变更**：所有库存变更必须通过统一的入库单/出库单处理，不能直接修改库存表

### 9.3 注意事项

1. **库存更新必须原子性**：扣减源仓库和增加目标仓库必须在同一事务中完成
2. **流水记录必须记录**：所有库存变动都必须记录到 `bill_inventory_item` 表
3. **版本号必须递增**：每次更新成功后，`version` 字段必须 +1
4. **重试机制**：对于并发冲突，建议实现重试机制（最多3次）
5. **性能优化**：对于高频查询，考虑使用 Redis 缓存
6. **统一抽象层（代码层，数据库无统一单据表）**：
   - 所有业务单据（采购入库单、调拨单、销售出库单、批次调整等）在代码层必须转换为统一入库/出库上下文（InventoryUnifiedInboundContext / InventoryUnifiedOutboundContext）
   - 统一库存更新服务仅接受上下文，是库存变更的唯一入口；流水写入 bill_inventory_item
   - 新增业务单据类型时，通过「上下文构建器 + 注册表」扩展，无需修改统一库存更新逻辑（详见 5.2.5）
7. **批次约束**：
   - 同批次仅限同一商品及同一仓库
   - 批次创建时，从入库单明细的池内可用数量中分配
   - 批次库存调整必须通过统一入库单/出库单处理

---

## 附录

### A. 状态枚举定义

#### A.1 入库单状态

| 状态码 | 状态名称 | 说明 |
|:------|:--------|:----|
| `DRAFT` | 📝 草稿 | 入库单创建后的初始状态 |
| `PENDING` | ⏳ 待审核 | 入库单已提交，等待审核 |
| `APPROVED` | ✅ 已审核 | 入库单审核通过 |
| `INBOUNDED` | 📥 已入库 | 入库操作完成，库存已更新 |
| `CANCELLED` | ❌ 已取消 | 入库单已取消 |

#### A.2 调拨单状态

| 状态码 | 状态名称 | 说明 |
|:------|:--------|:----|
| `DRAFT` | 📝 草稿 | 创建和提交后均为草稿状态，不更新库存 |
| `IN_TRANSIT` | 🚚 运输中 | 审核出库后，源仓库库存已扣减 |
| `COMPLETED` | ✅ 已完成 | 审核入库后，目标仓库库存已增加 |
| `CANCELLED` | ❌ 已取消 | 调拨单已取消 |

#### A.3 批次状态

| 状态码 | 状态名称 | 说明 |
|:------|:--------|:----|
| `ON_SHELF` | ✅ 已上架 | 批次发布即生效，无草稿状态 |
| `OFF_SHELF` | ❌ 已下架 | 批次作废，库存已返还到可用库存池 |

#### A.4 业务类型

| 业务类型码 | 业务类型名称 | 说明 |
|:----------|:-----------|:----|
| `PURCHASE_IN` | 📥 采购入库 | 采购商品入库操作 |
| `TRANSFER_IN` | 📥 调拨入库 | 调拨商品入库操作 |
| `TRANSFER_OUT` | 📤 调拨出库 | 调拨商品出库操作 |
| `SALES_OUT` | 📤 销售出库 | 销售商品出库操作 |
| `INVENTORY_ADJUSTMENT` | 🔧 库存盘点 | 库存盘点调整操作 |
| `BATCH_CREATE` | 🏷️ 批次创建 | 批次创建操作 |
| `BATCH_ADJUSTMENT` | 🔧 批次库存调整 | 批次库存调整操作 |
| `ALLOCATE` | 🔒 分配 | 库存分配操作 |
| `DEALLOCATE` | 🔓 取消分配 | 取消库存分配操作 |

#### A.5 批次业务动作
- `批次创建`: 批次创建时的初始库存
- `订单扣减`: 订单出库时扣减批次库存
- `批次调整`: 批次库存调整
- `纳入新单据`: 纳入新的入库单资源

---

## 附录

```java
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class UnifiedOrderServiceImpl implements UnifiedOrderService {
    
    private final UnifiedInboundOrderRepository unifiedInboundOrderRepository;
    private final UnifiedOutboundOrderRepository unifiedOutboundOrderRepository;
    private final InventoryRepository inventoryRepository;
    private final InventoryItemRepository inventoryItemRepository;
    
    /**
     * 通过统一入库单增加库存
     * 核心逻辑：更新库存表 + 记录库存流水（包含原始业务类型）
     */
    @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
    @Override
    public void increaseStockByUnifiedInbound(Long unifiedInboundOrderId) {
        // 1. 查询统一入库单
        UnifiedInboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = unifiedInboundOrderRepository.selectById(unifiedInboundOrderId);
        if (unifiedOrder == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("统一入库单不存在");
        }
        
        // 2. 查询统一入库单明细（包含业务类型和原始单据信息）
        List<UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity> items = unifiedInboundOrderRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(unifiedInboundOrderId);
        
        // 3. 对每个明细项更新库存并记录流水
        for (UnifiedInboundOrderItemEntity item : items) {
            // 3.1 查询当前库存
            InventoryQueryRequest queryRequest = new InventoryQueryRequest();
            queryRequest.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
            queryRequest.setWarehouseId(unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId());
            queryRequest.setProductStatus(ProductStatusEnum.NORMAL.getCode());
            InventoryEntity inventory = inventoryRepository.selectBySkuAndWarehouse(queryRequest);
            
            if (inventory == null) {
                // 创建新库存记录
                inventory = createNewInventory(item, unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId());
            }
            
            // 3.2 更新库存（带乐观锁）
            InventoryEntity updateEntity = new InventoryEntity();
            updateEntity.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
            updateEntity.setWarehouseId(unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId());
            updateEntity.setProductStatus(ProductStatusEnum.NORMAL.getCode());
            updateEntity.setVersion(inventory.getVersion());
            updateEntity.setChangeQuantity(item.getQuantity());
            
            int updateCount = inventoryRepository.updateStockWithVersion(updateEntity);
            if (updateCount == 0) {
                throw new ConcurrentModificationException("库存更新失败，请重试");
            }
            
            // 3.3 重新查询更新后的库存（获取最新版本和数量）
            InventoryEntity updatedInventory = inventoryRepository.selectBySkuAndWarehouse(queryRequest);
            
            // 3.4 记录库存流水（关键：保存原始业务类型和单据信息）
            InventoryItemEntity itemLog = new InventoryItemEntity();
            itemLog.setProductId(item.getProductId());
            itemLog.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
            itemLog.setWarehouseId(unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId());
            itemLog.setWarehouseName(getWarehouseName(unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId()));
            itemLog.setProductStatus(ProductStatusEnum.NORMAL.getCode());
            itemLog.setChangeTime(LocalDateTime.now());
            // 关键：使用统一入库单明细中的业务类型，而不是"统一入库"
            itemLog.setBusinessType(item.getBusinessType()); // PURCHASE_IN, TRANSFER_IN等
            itemLog.setRelatedDocumentType(item.getRelatedDocumentType()); // IN, TR等
            itemLog.setRelatedDocumentId(item.getRelatedDocumentId()); // IN-2023102401, TR-20231026001等
            itemLog.setChangeQuantity(item.getQuantity()); // 正数
            itemLog.setTotalBalanceAfterChange(updatedInventory.getTotalStock());
            itemLog.setOperatorId(getCurrentUserId());
            itemLog.setOperatorName(getCurrentUserName());
            
            inventoryItemRepository.insert(itemLog);
        }
    }
    
    /**
     * 通过统一出库单减少库存
     * 核心逻辑：更新库存表 + 记录库存流水（包含原始业务类型）
     */
    @Transactional(rollbackFor = Exception.class)
    @Override
    public void decreaseStockByUnifiedOutbound(Long unifiedOutboundOrderId) {
        // 1. 查询统一出库单
        UnifiedOutboundOrderEntity unifiedOrder = unifiedOutboundOrderRepository.selectById(unifiedOutboundOrderId);
        if (unifiedOrder == null) {
            throw new BusinessException("统一出库单不存在");
        }
        
        // 2. 查询统一出库单明细（包含业务类型和原始单据信息）
        List<UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity> items = unifiedOutboundOrderRepository.selectItemsByOrderId(unifiedOutboundOrderId);
        
        // 3. 对每个明细项更新库存并记录流水
        for (UnifiedOutboundOrderItemEntity item : items) {
            // 3.1 查询当前库存
            InventoryQueryRequest queryRequest = new InventoryQueryRequest();
            queryRequest.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
            queryRequest.setWarehouseId(unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId());
            queryRequest.setProductStatus(ProductStatusEnum.NORMAL.getCode());
            InventoryEntity inventory = inventoryRepository.selectBySkuAndWarehouse(queryRequest);
            
            if (inventory == null || inventory.getTotalStock() < item.getQuantity()) {
                throw new InsufficientStockException("库存不足");
            }
            
            // 3.2 更新库存（带乐观锁）
            InventoryEntity updateEntity = new InventoryEntity();
            updateEntity.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
            updateEntity.setWarehouseId(unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId());
            updateEntity.setProductStatus(ProductStatusEnum.NORMAL.getCode());
            updateEntity.setVersion(inventory.getVersion());
            updateEntity.setChangeQuantity(-item.getQuantity()); // 负数表示减少
            
            int updateCount = inventoryRepository.updateStockWithVersion(updateEntity);
            if (updateCount == 0) {
                throw new ConcurrentModificationException("库存更新失败，请重试");
            }
            
            // 3.3 重新查询更新后的库存
            InventoryEntity updatedInventory = inventoryRepository.selectBySkuAndWarehouse(queryRequest);
            
            // 3.4 记录库存流水（关键：保存原始业务类型和单据信息）
            InventoryItemEntity itemLog = new InventoryItemEntity();
            itemLog.setProductId(item.getProductId());
            itemLog.setSkuCode(item.getSkuCode());
            itemLog.setWarehouseId(unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId());
            itemLog.setWarehouseName(getWarehouseName(unifiedOrder.getWarehouseId()));
            itemLog.setProductStatus(ProductStatusEnum.NORMAL.getCode());
            itemLog.setChangeTime(LocalDateTime.now());
            // 关键：使用统一出库单明细中的业务类型，而不是"统一出库"
            itemLog.setBusinessType(item.getBusinessType()); // SALES_OUT, TRANSFER_OUT等
            itemLog.setRelatedDocumentType(item.getRelatedDocumentType()); // ORD, TR等
            itemLog.setRelatedDocumentId(item.getRelatedDocumentId()); // ORD-20231026-8891, TR-20231026001等
            itemLog.setChangeQuantity(-item.getQuantity()); // 负数表示减少
            itemLog.setTotalBalanceAfterChange(updatedInventory.getTotalStock());
            itemLog.setOperatorId(getCurrentUserId());
            itemLog.setOperatorName(getCurrentUserName());
            
            inventoryItemRepository.insert(itemLog);
        }
    }
}
```

### 11.4 库存流水查询和展示逻辑

```java
@Service
@RequiredArgsConstructor
public class InventoryItemServiceImpl implements InventoryItemService {
    
    private final InventoryItemRepository inventoryItemRepository;
    
    /**
     * 查询库存流水日志
     * 对外展示时，显示原始业务类型（采购入库、销售出库、调拨入库、调拨出库等）
     */
    @Override
    public IPage<InventoryItemDTO> queryItemLog(InventoryItemQueryRequest request) {
        // 1. 构建查询条件
        InventoryItemQueryRequest queryRequest = new InventoryItemQueryRequest();
        queryRequest.setSkuCode(request.getSkuCode());
        queryRequest.setWarehouseId(request.getWarehouseId());
        queryRequest.setBusinessType(request.getBusinessType()); // 可以按业务类型筛选
        queryRequest.setRelatedDocumentId(request.getRelatedDocumentId()); // 可以按单据号搜索
        queryRequest.setStartDate(request.getStartDate());
        queryRequest.setEndDate(request.getEndDate());
        
        // 2. 分页查询
        Page<InventoryItemEntity> page = new Page<>(request.getPageIndex(), request.getPageSize());
        IPage<InventoryItemEntity> entityPage = inventoryItemRepository.selectPage(page, queryRequest);
        
        // 3. 转换为DTO（业务类型转换为中文显示）
        IPage<InventoryItemDTO> dtoPage = entityPage.convert(entity -> {
            InventoryItemDTO dto = new InventoryItemDTO();
            dto.setId(entity.getId());
            dto.setChangeTime(entity.getChangeTime());
            // 关键：使用原始业务类型，转换为中文显示
            dto.setBusinessType(getBusinessTypeDisplayName(entity.getBusinessType()));
            dto.setRelatedDocumentType(entity.getRelatedDocumentType());
            dto.setRelatedDocumentId(entity.getRelatedDocumentId()); // 显示原始单据号
            dto.setWarehouseName(entity.getWarehouseName());
            dto.setChangeQuantity(entity.getChangeQuantity());
            dto.setTotalBalanceAfterChange(entity.getTotalBalanceAfterChange());
            dto.setOperatorName(entity.getOperatorName());
            return dto;
        });
        
        return dtoPage;
    }
    
    /**
     * 业务类型转换为中文显示名称
     */
    private String getBusinessTypeDisplayName(String businessType) {
        switch (businessType) {
            case "PURCHASE_IN":
                return "采购入库";
            case "TRANSFER_IN":
                return "调拨入库";
            case "TRANSFER_OUT":
                return "调拨出库";
            case "SALES_OUT":
                return "销售出库";
            case "BATCH_ADJUSTMENT":
                return "批次调整";
            case "INVENTORY_ADJUSTMENT":
                return "库存盘点";
            default:
                return businessType;
        }
    }
}
```

### 11.5 核心流程总结

```mermaid
flowchart LR
    subgraph Business["业务单据"]
        A[采购入库单]
        B[调拨单]
        C[销售出库单]
        D[批次调整]
    end
    
    subgraph Convert["转换"]
        E[统一入库/出库上下文<br/>代码层，不落统一表]
    end
    
    subgraph Context["上下文"]
        F[包含业务类型<br/>单据号、仓库、明细]
    end
    
    subgraph Inventory["库存"]
        G[更新 inventory<br/>写流水 bill_inventory_item]
    end
    
    subgraph Display["展示"]
        H[显示原始业务类型]
    end
    
    A & B & C & D --> E --> F --> G --> H
    
    style Business fill:#fff9c4
    style Convert fill:#e1f5ff
    style Context fill:#e8f5e9
    style Inventory fill:#c8e6c9
    style Display fill:#f3e5f5
```

### 11.6 关键设计要点

1. **统一入库/出库上下文（代码层）必须包含业务追溯字段**
   - `business_type`、`bill_type`、`bill_id`、`bill_code` 等，写流水时写入 `bill_inventory_item`

2. **库存流水写入 bill_inventory_item，从上下文中取业务信息**
   - 不记录"统一入库"或"统一出库"，而是记录原始业务类型（采购入库、销售出库、调拨入库、调拨出库等）
   - 数据库层无统一单据表，流水表承载追溯信息

3. **对外展示时使用库存流水中的业务类型**
   - 前端查询库存流水时，显示原始业务类型
   - 用户看到的是"采购入库单增加了库存"，而不是"统一入库单增加了库存"

4. **追溯完整**
   - 通过 `bill_code`、`bill_id` 可追溯到原始业务单据
   - 通过 `business_type` 可区分不同业务场景

5. **扩展性**：新增业务单据时，通过「上下文构建器 + 注册表」扩展，不修改统一库存服务（详见 5.2.5、8.1.8）。

---

</div>
